[[from_formal_language]]
== From Formal Language


AsciiDoc è¯­è¨€è§„èŒƒç›®æ ‡æ—¨åœ¨ä¿ƒè¿›è·¨ä¸åŒç¼–ç¨‹è¯­è¨€å’Œè¿è¡Œæ—¶å¼€å‘å…¼å®¹çš„ AsciiDoc æ ¼å¼å®ç°ã€‚
ä¸ºäº†é¿å…åœ¨ä¸åŒè¯­è¨€å®ç°ä¸­ä¸å¿…è¦åœ°é‡å†™æµ‹è¯•ï¼ŒAsciiDoc ä¾ç…§ Eclipse åŸºé‡‘ä¼šè§„èŒƒè¿‡ç¨‹ï¼Œ
ä¸ºè§„èŒƒé¡¹ç›®ç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªæŠ€æœ¯å…¼å®¹æ€§å·¥å…·åŒ…ï¼ˆTechnology Compatibility Kit, TCKï¼‰ï¼Œ
è¯¥å·¥å…·åŒ…æ‰¿è¯ºå®ç°å¤šä¸ªå…¼å®¹çš„å®ç°ã€‚TCK çš„ä½œç”¨æ˜¯ç¡®ä¿å®ç°çš„å…¼å®¹æ€§å’Œåº”ç”¨ç¨‹åºçš„å¯ç§»æ¤æ€§ã€‚
æƒ³è¦è·å¾—è®¤è¯çš„å®ç°å¿…é¡»éµå¾ª AsciiDoc TCK æµç¨‹ã€‚

AsciiDoc è¯­è¨€æ ¸å¿ƒæ˜¯æ¯”æŠ½è±¡è¯­æ³•æ ‘ (Abstract Syntax Tree, AST) è¿˜æ›´é«˜æŠ½è±¡æ°´å¹³çš„
æŠ½è±¡è¯­ä¹‰å›¾ (Abstract Semantic Graph, ASG)ï¼Œè¿™æ˜¯å› ä¸º AsciiDoc ç”¨äºå¤„ç†æ–‡æ¡£çš„
ç»“æ„ï¼Œè€Œéç”¨äºé€šç”¨ç¼–ç¨‹ã€‚è¿™ä¸€ç‚¹ä¸ Pandoc è¿™ä¸ªå¼€æºçš„æ–‡æ¡£æ ¼å¼è½¬æ¢å·¥å…·ç±»ä¼¼ï¼Œå®ƒä»¬éƒ½ä½¿ç”¨
JSON ä½œä¸ºæ–‡æ¡£æ ¼å¼ä¿¡æ¯çš„å­˜å‚¨åª’ä»‹ã€‚ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯ Wikipedia ä¸­å®šä¹‰çš„ ASG æ¦‚å¿µ:

____
An is a form of abstract syntax in which an expression of a formal 
or programming language is represented by a graph whose vertices are 
the expressionâ€™s subterms. An ASG is at a higher level of abstraction 
than an, which is used to express the syntactic structure of an 
expression or program.
____

è®¡ç®—æœºè¯­è¨€é¢†åŸŸä¸Šè®²ï¼ŒAsciiDoc å¹¶ä¸åƒ XML è¿™ç±»æ­£åˆ™è¯­è¨€ï¼ˆregular languageï¼‰é‚£æ ·ï¼Œ
å¯ä»¥æ ¹æ®ä¸€ä¸ªè¯­è¨€è§„èŒƒæ¥è¿›è¡Œæ•°æ®å¤„ç†ï¼Œä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯è¯´ AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£æ˜¯ä¸€ç§æ²¡æœ‰å›ºå®šæ­£åˆ™è§„èŒƒ
çš„æ ¼å¼ï¼ŒAsciiDoc ASG å°±æ˜¯ç”¨äºæ•è·æˆ–è€…è¡¨ç° AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£å†…éƒ¨ç»“æ„çš„å±‚æ¬¡æ¨¡å‹ã€‚

è™½ç„¶è¯´ ASG æ¯” AST æŠ½è±¡ç­‰çº§è¿˜è¦é«˜ï¼Œå¥½åƒä¼šæ›´éš¾ç†è§£ï¼Œä½†å…¶å®ä¸ç„¶ï¼Œå®ƒçš„æ¨¡å¼å®šä¹‰æ–‡ä»¶æ›´æ˜“æ‡‚ã€‚
ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯è§„èŒƒæ–‡æ¡£ä¸­ç»™å‡ºçš„ ASG schema ä¸æµ‹è¯•æ ·å¼æ•°æ®ã€‚æ­£æ–‡æ®µè½çš„ ASG schema æ˜¯æŠ½è±¡è¯­æ³•
æ ‘ä¸Šçš„å¶å—ï¼ˆleaf blockï¼‰ï¼Œä¹Ÿæ˜¯æŠ½è±¡å—å¯¹è±¡çš„æ‰©å±•ï¼Œå®ƒçš„æ¨¡å¼å®šä¹‰åœ¨å®˜æ–¹æ–‡æ¡£çš„ ASG
æ–‡ä»¶å¤¹ä¸­ schema.json ä¸­æè¿°ï¼š

.ASG schema
[source,json]
-------------
"paragraph": {
  "type": "object",
  "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractBlock" }],
  "unevaluatedProperties": false,
  "required": ["name"],
  "defaults": { "inlines": [] },
  "properties": {
    "name": { "type": "string", "constant": "paragraph" },
    "form": { "type": "string", "enum": "paragraph" },
    "inlines": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlines" }
  }
}
-------------

.ASG example of an ASG node for a paragraph
[source,json]
-------------
{
  "name": "paragraph",
  "type": "block",
  "inlines": [
    {
      "name": "text",
      "type": "string",
      "value": "This paragraph has multiple lines that wrap after reaching the 72\ncharacter limit.",
      "location": [{ "line": 1, "col": 1 }, { "line": 2, "col": 16 }]
    }
  ],
  "location": [{ "line": 1, "col": 1 }, { "line": 2, "col": 16 }]
}
-------------

.abstractBlock from ASG schema.json.
[source,json]
-------------
    "abstractBlock": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["type"],
      "properties": {
        "type": { "type": "string", "const": "block" },
        "id": { "type": "string" },
        "title": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlines" },
        "reftext": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlines" },
        "metadata": { "$ref": "#/$defs/blockMetadata" },
        "location": { "$ref": "#/$defs/location" }
      }
    },
-------------

åœ¨æ¨¡å¼å®šä¹‰æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­ï¼Œå¯ä»¥çœ‹åˆ° `leafBlock` å’Œ `parentBlock` ä¸¤ä¸ªæ–‡æ¡£å¯¹è±¡ç±»å‹å·²ç»æ¶µç›–æ—¥å¸¸ä½¿ç”¨çš„
å¤§éƒ¨åˆ†æ–‡æ¡£å…ƒç´ ç±»å‹ã€‚å…¶ä¸­ï¼Œä»£ç å—ï¼ˆlisting Blockï¼‰ä¹‹æ‰€ä»¥å’Œæ®µè½ï¼ˆparagraphï¼‰éƒ½åˆ’åˆ†åˆ° 
leafBlockï¼Œä¸»è¦ä¸€ä¸ªåŸå› æ˜¯å®ƒåŒ…å«çš„å†…å®¹æ˜¯ç›´é€šè¾“å‡ºçš„ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸éœ€è¦åšå¤§é‡çš„å†…å®¹æ›¿æ¢æ“ä½œã€‚


<<<
[reftext="è¡¨è¾¾å¼è§£ææ–‡æ³•ï¼ˆPEGï¼‰"]
[[parsing_expression_grammars]]
== Parsing Expression Grammars

è®¡ç®—æœºè¯­è¨€ç¼–è¯‘è½¯ä»¶çš„å®ç°æŠ€æœ¯ä¸Šï¼Œå¤§ä½“å¯ä»¥æ ¹æ®æ„é€ åˆ†ææƒçš„å½¢å¼åˆ†ä¸ºä¸¤ç±»ï¼šè‡ªé¡¶å‘ä¸‹æ„å»ºåˆ†ææ ‘ã€
ä»¥åŠè‡ªåº•å‘ä¸Šæ„å»ºåˆ†ææ ‘ã€‚è¿™ä¸¤ç§æ–¹å¼å¯¹åº”çš„ç®—æ³•åˆ†ç±»æ˜¯ LL ç³»ç®—æ³•å’Œ LR ç³»ç®—æ³•ã€‚

LL Parser å®ç°ä»£ç çš„ç»“æ„ä¸æ–‡æ³•å¯¹åº”ï¼Œæ˜“ç†è§£ï¼Œé”™è¯¯å¤„ç†å’Œé”™è¯¯æ¢å¤ä¹Ÿå¥½å¤„ç†ã€‚å½“å‰è¾ƒæœ‰ä»£è¡¨æ€§çš„æ˜¯ PEG
(Parse Expression Grammar)ï¼Œè¿™ç§è‡ªä¸‹è€Œä¸‹çš„ã€çº¿æ€§åˆ†æå™¨å¾ˆå¥½åœ°è§£å†³äº†è‡ªä¸Šè€Œä¸‹çš„äºŒä¹‰é€‰æ‹©é—®é¢˜ã€‚
PEG æ–‡æ³•é€šè¿‡å¼•å…¥ Prioritized choice operator â€˜/â€™ æ¥æä¾›éäºŒä¹‰çš„é€‰æ‹©ï¼Œå³æœ‰é™å›æº¯çš„æ–‡æ³•ã€‚
è€Œæµè¡Œçš„ç”Ÿæˆå™¨å·¥å…·ï¼ŒANTLR 3 æˆ–è€… ANTLR 4 å°±æ˜¯é‡‡ç”¨ LL ç³»åˆ—ç®—æ³•è‡ªåŠ¨ç”Ÿæˆè§£é‡Šå™¨çš„å·¥å…·ã€‚

LR Parser è™½ç„¶å®ç°ä¸Šæ›´å¤æ‚ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯å…¶é€Ÿåº¦å¿«ã€è¡¨è¾¾èƒ½åŠ›å¼ºã€‚å› æ­¤ï¼ŒæŒæ¡ LR åˆ†ææ–¹æ³•æ¯” LL æ›´å…·æœ‰å®æ“æ„ä¹‰ã€‚

å‚è€ƒèµ„æ–™ï¼šlink:http://staff.ustc.edu.cn/~yuzhang/compiler/2022f/lectures/03-parsing-part3-antlr.pdf[è¯­æ³•åˆ†æ III, ä¸­å›½ç§‘å¤§ å¼ æ˜±]

PEG (Parsing Expression Grammars) è¡¨è¾¾å¼è§£æè¯­æ³•å¯ä»¥è§£æä¸€é—¨ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡æ— å…³è¯­è¨€ï¼Œ
åŒ…æ‹¬é€’å½’ç»“æ„ã€‚ä»è¯­è¨€å®ç°æ–¹å¼æ¥è¯´ï¼Œç±»ä¼¼ Yacc æˆ– Bison è¿™æ ·çš„å·¥å…·æ¥å®ç°è§£é‡Šå™¨ã€‚
PEG æ˜¯ç”¨å­—ç¬¦ä¸²åŒ¹é… (pattern) æ¥æè¿°è¯­è¨€çš„æ–¹å¼ï¼Œä¹Ÿå³è¡¨è¾¾å¼è§£æè¿™ç§è¡Œä¸ºæ˜¯å…¶çš„æ ¸å¿ƒã€‚
PEG çš„å®ç°ä¸Šä¸ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡æ— æ³•æ–‡æ³• context free grammars (CFGs) çš„å®ç°éå¸¸ä¸åŒã€‚
PEG ä¸ç®€åŒ–ä¸ºçŠ¶æ€æœºï¼Œè€Œæ˜¯é‡‡ç”¨é¡ºåºè§£æã€‚è¿™æ„å‘³ç€ç¼–å†™è§£æè§„åˆ™çš„é¡ºåºå¾ˆé‡è¦ã€‚
PEG å¯ä»¥æ›´å®¹æ˜“ç¼–å†™ã€‚é€šå¸¸ä¸éœ€è¦ç¼–å†™å•ç‹¬æ–‡æ¡£æµçš„æ‰«æç¨‹åºï¼Œè¯­æ³•ï¼ˆæ–‡æ³•ï¼‰ç›´æ¥ä¸è¾“å…¥
æ–‡æœ¬ä¸€èµ·å·¥ä½œï¼Œè€Œä¸éœ€è¦ Tokenization æ­¥éª¤ã€‚

AsciiDoc å±äºä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡æ— å…³çš„è¯­è¨€ã€‚è§£æ AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£ä¸èƒ½æœ‰æ­§ä¹‰ï¼Œè¿™æ„å‘³ç€åªæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªæœ‰æ•ˆ

To cite https://blog.reverberate.org/2013/09/ll-and-lr-in-context-why-parsing-tools.html:

> Parsing expression grammars avoid ambiguity by forcing all grammar rules to be defined in terms of prioritized choice.

.Test cases from {Test_ALT130}
:Test_ALT130: link:https://vscode.dev/github.com/asciidoctor/asciidoctor/blob/main/test/attribute_list_test.rb#L130-L152[attribute_list_test.rb Line #130]
[source,rb]
-----------
  test 'collect unnamed attribute enclosed in equal signs' do
    attributes = {}
    line = '=foo='
    expected = { 1 => '=foo=' }
    (Asciidoctor::AttributeList.new line).parse_into attributes
    assert_equal expected, attributes
  end

  test 'collect named attribute' do
    attributes = {}
    line = 'foo=bar'
    expected = { 'foo' => 'bar' }
    (Asciidoctor::AttributeList.new line).parse_into attributes
    assert_equal expected, attributes
  end

  test 'collect named attribute double-quoted' do
    attributes = {}
    line = 'foo="bar"'
    expected = { 'foo' => 'bar' }
    (Asciidoctor::AttributeList.new line).parse_into attributes
    assert_equal expected, attributes
  end
-----------

æ’ä»¶è¿˜æä¾›äº†ä¸€ç»„ snippets (snippets.json) ä»£ç ç‰‡æ®µï¼Œåªéœ€è¦è¾“å…¥ä»¥ä¸‹ç¼©å†™ï¼Œå¹¶æŒ‰ Ctrl+Space
å°±å¯ä»¥è¾“å…¥ç›¸åº”çš„ä»£ç æ¨¡æ¿ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ä»¥ä¸‹è¡¨æ ¼å°±å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ "table" ä»£ç ç‰‡æ®µæ¥å¿«é€Ÿå®ŒæˆåŸºæœ¬ç»“æ„çš„è¾“å…¥ï¼š

[cols="2,4s",width="80%"]
|===
|Snippet prefix       |Snippet body and note

|"asciidoc-tech-doc"  | An AsciiDoc outline
|"include"            | include::path[attributes]
|"image"              | "\image:${1:path}[${2:alt}]"
|"image"              | "image::${1:path}[${2:alt}]"
|"video"              | "video::${1:path}[${2:alt}]"
|"link"               | "\link:${1:${TM_SELECTED_TEXT:link}}[${2:alt}]"
|"mailto"             | "\mailto:${1:${TM_SELECTED_TEXT:link}}[${2:alt}]"
|"header"             | Document Title, Author, version...
|"heading"            | ${1\|=,==,===,====,=====,======\|} ${2:${TM_SELECTED_TEXT:Heading Title}}
|"unordered list"     | ["* ${1:first}", "* ${2:second}", "* ${3:third}", "$0"]
|"ordered list"       | [". ${1:first}", ". ${2:second}", ". ${3:third}", "$0"]
|"checklist"          | * [${1: }] ${2:first} ...
|"literal"            | [${1:attributes}]\n....\n${2:${TM_SELECTED_TEXT:text}}\n.... 
|"source"             | [source,${1:language},${2:attributes}]\n----\n...----\n
|"example"            | [${1:attributes}]\n====\n...\n====
|"sidebar"            | [${1:attributes}]\n****\n...\n****
|"table"              | [${1:Attributes}]\n\|===\n...\n\|===
|"tag"                | // tag::${1:tagname}[]\n...\n// end::${1:tagname}[]
|"quote"              | [quote, ${1:attribution}, ${2:cite title}]\n____\n...\n____
|"footnote"           | "\footnote:[${1:note}]"
|"footnote-label"     | "footnote:${1:label}[${2:note}]"
|===

SDR4 æ–‡æ¡£è¡¨ç¤ºï¼Œä¸ºäº†ä»¥å®ç°åˆç†å‘åå…¼å®¹æ€§çš„æ–¹å¼æè¿° AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£ç»“æ„ä½¿ç”¨äº†å¤šç§è¯­æ³•
ï¼ˆMultiple grammarsï¼‰ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬

* line preprocessor è¡Œå†…å®¹é¢„å¤„ç†ç¨‹åº (å¯èƒ½æ•´åˆåˆ° block)
* block å—å†…å®¹
* attrlist å±æ€§åˆ—è¡¨
* inline preprocessor å†…è”å†…å®¹é¢„å¤„ç†ç¨‹åº
* inline å†…è”å†…å®¹


å˜æ›´æ—¥å¿—ï¼ˆCHANGELOG.adocï¼‰è®°å½•äº†ä» 0.2.0 åˆ° 0.3.0 è¿™ä¸¤ä¸ªä¸»è¦æ›´æ–°æ‰€å¸¦æ¥çš„æ–‡æ¡£ï¼š

. 0.3.0 (milestone build)
* Draft section in specification for paragraph (#35)
* Draft section in specification for strong span (#37)
* SDR-6: Define Parsing Rules for Positional Attribute to Named Attribute Mapping (#36)
* SDR 7: Designate List Continuation as Universal Interrupting Line (#42)
* SDR 8: Designate List Item as Interrupting Line only for Principal Text (#42)

. 0.2.0 (milestone build)
* Selected JSON as the format for the ASG used by the TCK (#7)
* Create initial draft of JSON schema for the ASG; resides in the asg folder (#28)
* SDR-1: Introduce variable-length delimiter form for open block (#27)
* SDR-2: Define parsing and aggregation rules for attrlist in block attribute line (and block macros) (#33)
* SDR-3: Clarify that block style does not influence parsing model, but is rather a parsing transformation (#31)
* SDR-4: Select PEG as the grammar formalism for describing the AsciiDoc language (#8)
* SDR-5: Transition the inline syntax to a formal grammar from a substitutions step; introduce an inline preprocessor (#16, #22)

LPeg (Parsing Expression Grammars for Lua) è¢«è®¾è®¡å‡ºæ¥ç”¨äºè§£æè¯­æ³•ï¼Œé€šè¿‡
å®ƒèƒ½å¤Ÿè½»æ¾åœ°è§£æå„ç§è¯­æ³•ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ {lua-parser} ç”¨äº”ç™¾è¡Œä»£ç å°† Lua ä»£ç è§£ææˆæŠ½è±¡
è¯­æ³•æ ‘ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ç‚¹å‡» {lua-parser-dev} æŸ¥çœ‹å…¶ä»£ç ã€‚LPeg ä½œä¸ºè¯­è¨€å·¥å…·ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ç”¨å®ƒæ¥
åšä»£ç çš„é™æ€åˆ†æï¼Œè‡ªå®šä¹‰é¢†åŸŸè¯­è¨€ (DSL, Domain Specific Language)ï¼Œå°†æ˜“å¦‚åæŒã€‚

ä¾‹å¦‚åœ¨æ¸¸æˆç¼–ç¨‹ä¸­ï¼Œç­–åˆ’å¸¸å¸¸éœ€è¦é…ç½®è§¦å‘å™¨ï¼Œè§¦å‘æ¡ä»¶æœ‰æ—¶æ¯”è¾ƒå¤æ‚ï¼Œç¼–ç¨‹å®ç°æ¯”è¾ƒç¹çã€‚
æ¯”å¦‚ â€œè¡€é‡å°äº 10% æˆ–æ€’æ°”å¤§äº 90 æ—¶æœ‰ 50% çš„æ¦‚ç‡è§¦å‘â€ã€‚è¿™ç§åœºæ™¯å°±å¯ä»¥è‡ªå®šä¹‰
DSL, é…ç½®è¡¨åªç”¨æ¥è®¾ç½®å¯ä»¥é…ç½®çš„é¢„å®šä¹‰å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼ˆhp, wrath, randomï¼‰ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆä»¥ä¸Š
è¿™ä¸ªæ¡ä»¶å°±å¯ä»¥ç”¨å­—ç¬¦ä¸²è¡¨ç¤ºä¸ºä»¥ä¸‹è¿™æ ·çš„è¯­å¥ã€‚ç„¶åä½¿ç”¨ LPeg å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç¼–è¯‘æˆä¸€ä¸ª

.DSL statement
=====
  (hp < 10% || wrath > 90) && random() > 0.5
=====

Lua æ–‡æ¡£çš„ The Complete Syntax of Lua ä¸€ç« å†…å®¹æ˜¯ BNF (Backus Naur Form) 
èŒƒå¼æè¿°çš„ Lua è¯­è¨€è¯­æ³•ã€‚BNF å°±æ˜¯ CFG çš„ä¸€ç§è¡¨ç¤ºæ³•. è¯­æ³•éå¸¸ç®€çŸ­ï¼Œåªæœ‰ 67 è¡Œè§„åˆ™ã€‚
ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯ Lua 5.3 è¯­è¨€çš„æ–‡æ³•æè¿°ï¼Œä¸ Lua 5ã€‚4 å·®å¦åœ¨å°† `namelist` æ›´æ–°ä¸º `attnamelist`ã€‚

.BNF of Lua 5.3
[source,BNF]
------------
    chunk ::= block

    block ::= {stat} [retstat]

    stat ::=  ';' | 
         varlist '=' explist | 
         functioncall | 
         label | 
         break | 
         goto Name | 
         do block end | 
         while exp do block end | 
         repeat block until exp | 
         if exp then block {elseif exp then block} [else block] end | 
         for Name '=' exp ',' exp [',' exp] do block end | 
         for namelist in explist do block end | 
         function funcname funcbody | 
         local function Name funcbody | 
         local namelist ['=' explist] 

    retstat ::= return [explist] [';']

    label ::= '::' Name '::'

    funcname ::= Name {'.' Name} [':' Name]

    varlist ::= var {',' var}

    var ::=  Name | prefixexp '[' exp ']' | prefixexp '.' Name 

    namelist ::= Name {',' Name}

    explist ::= exp {',' exp}

    exp ::=  nil | false | true | Numeral | LiteralString | '...' | functiondef | 
         prefixexp | tableconstructor | exp binop exp | unop exp 

    prefixexp ::= var | functioncall | '(' exp ')'

    functioncall ::=  prefixexp args | prefixexp ':' Name args 

    args ::=  '(' [explist] ')' | tableconstructor | LiteralString 

    functiondef ::= function funcbody

    funcbody ::= '(' [parlist] ')' block end

    parlist ::= namelist [',' '...'] | '...'

    tableconstructor ::= '{' [fieldlist] '}'

    fieldlist ::= field {fieldsep field} [fieldsep]

    field ::= '[' exp ']' '=' exp | Name '=' exp | exp

    fieldsep ::= ',' | ';'

    binop ::= '+' | '-' | '*' | '/' | '//' | '^' | '%' | 
              '&' | '~' | '|' | '>>' | '<<' | '..' | 
              '<' | '<=' | '>' | '>=' | '==' | '~=' | 
              and | or

    unop  ::= '-' | not | '#' | '~'
------------

.BNF update of Lua 5.4
[source,BNF]
------------
    stat ::=  ';' | 
         ...
         local namelist ['=' explist]   <.>
         local attnamelist ['=' explist] <.>

    attnamelist ::=  Name attrib {',' Name attrib}

    attrib ::= ['<' Name '>']
    ...
------------
<.> Different part come from Lua 5.3
<.> Different part come from Lua 5.4


ä¸‹é¢æ˜¯ç”¨ PEG å¯¹å…¶è¯­æ³•çš„è‡ªæè¿°ï¼Œè¯­æ³•è§„åˆ™æ›´çŸ­å°:

[source,BNF]
------------
1  grammar     <-  (nonterminal â€™<-â€™ sp pattern)+
2  pattern     <-  alternative (â€™/â€™ sp alternative)*
3  alternative <-  ([!&]? sp suffix)+
4  suffix      <-  primary ([*+?] sp)*
5  primary     <-  â€™(â€™ sp pattern â€™)â€™ sp / â€™.â€™ sp / literal /
6                  charclass / nonterminal !â€™<-â€™
7  literal     <-  [â€™] (![â€™] .)* [â€™] sp
8  charclass   <-  â€™[â€™ (!â€™]â€™ (. â€™-â€™ . / .))* â€™]â€™ sp
9  nonterminal <-  [a-zA-Z]+ sp
10 sp          <-  [ \t\n]*
------------

ç¬¬ 1 è¡Œè¡¨ç¤º PEG è¯­æ³•ç”±ä¸€æ¡ä»¥ä¸Šçš„è§„åˆ™ç»„æˆ, æ¯æ¡è§„åˆ™çš„ <- å·¦ä¾§ä¸ºéç»ˆç»“ç¬¦ (nonterminal)ï¼Œ
å³ä¾§ä¸ºæ¨¡å¼ (pattern)ï¼Œå¯¹åº”ä¸‹ä¸€çº§ nonterminalã€‚è¿™äº›è§„åˆ™å¯ä»¥é€æ¡æ¨å¯¼ï¼Œç›´åˆ°å­—ç¬¦çº§åˆ«ï¼Œå³

è¿™æ¡è§„åˆ™å°±ä¸ä¼šå†å›æº¯ï¼ˆæœ‰é™å›æº¯ï¼‰ã€‚å‡å®š E2 ä½œä¸º A è§„åˆ™çš„æˆåŠŸåŒ¹é…é¡¹ï¼Œå¦‚æœæ¥ä¸‹æ¥ S è§„åˆ™ä¸­çš„

PEG çš„æ•ˆç‡ï¼Œä¸ä¼šå‡ºç°æ­£åˆ™è¡¨è¾¾å¼ä¸€æ ·çš„æ— é™å›æº¯çš„é—®é¢˜ã€‚

è´ªå©ªåŒ¹é… (greedy match) ä¸æ‡’æƒ°åŒ¹é…ï¼ˆlazy matchï¼‰æ˜¯æ­£åˆ™è¯­è¨€å¸¸è§ç”¨æ³•ã€‚æ¯”å¦‚ `pass:[.*]` 
ä¼šåŒ¹é…ä»»æ„é•¿åº¦ï¼ˆ`+*+`ï¼‰çš„ä»»æ„å­—ç¬¦ï¼ˆ`.`ï¼‰ã€‚ç±»ä¼¼åœ°ï¼Œ`pass:[.*e]` ä¼šåŒ¹é…ä»»æ„ä»¥ `e` ç»“å°¾
çš„ä»»æ„é•¿åº¦çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚åœ¨åŒ¹é…å­—ç¬¦æ—¶ï¼Œå°±ç®—æ‰¾åˆ° `e` ä¹Ÿä¼šç»§ç»­å†å¾€ä¸‹æ‰¾ï¼Œç›´åˆ°ç»“æŸå‘ç°æ²¡æœ‰æ›´å¤š
æ‰å›æº¯åˆ°å‰é¢ã€‚è¿™ç§æ— é™çš„å›æº¯èƒ½åŠ›å ªç§°ç¾éš¾æ€§å›æº¯ï¼ˆCatastrophic Backtrackingï¼‰ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨
ä¸å½“æœ‰å¯èƒ½å¯¼è‡´è½¯ä»¶ä¸èƒ½ç»§ç»­æä¾›æœåŠ¡ã€‚å¦‚æœæ˜¯ `.*?e` å°±ä¼šè¿›å…¥æ‡’æƒ°åŒ¹é…æ¨¡å¼ï¼Œåªè¦é‡åˆ° `e`

å¹¶ä¸”ä¸è€ƒè™‘å‰åçš„å…¶ä»–æ¨¡å¼ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚ï¼Œå¦‚ä¸‹çš„ PEG è§„åˆ™ï¼š

[source,BNF,role="warmlens"]
============================
S1   <-  .* â€™Xâ€™

S2   <-  (!â€™Xâ€™ .)* â€™Xâ€™

S3   <-  â€™Xâ€™ / . S3

== ASG schema.json

jq æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªè½»é‡çº§ JSON æ•°æ®å¤„ç†ç¨‹åºï¼Œå¯ä»¥ç”¨å®ƒæ¥å¤„ç† ASG schema ä¸­çš„æ•°æ®ç»“æ„ï¼Œ
å‚è€ƒ link:jq-1.7-doc.adoc[jq æ•™ç¨‹åŠæ‰‹å†Œ]ã€‚åŒç±»å½¢å·¥å…·ä¸­è¿˜æœ‰ Miller (mlr)ï¼Œ
è¿™æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªé›†æ•°æ®è¯¢ã€æ•´å½¢ã€é‡æ„æ ¼å¼ï¼ˆåŒ…æ‹¬åˆ¶ä½œï¼‰çš„å‘½ä»¤è¡Œå·¥å…·ï¼Œæ”¯æŒ CSV, TSV, JSON,

å¯ä»¥è®¾ç½®å„ç§ UML å…³ç³»ç®­å¤´ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯æ²¡æœ‰æä¾›å„å±æ€§é—´çš„è¿çº¿ã€ç®­å¤´åŠŸèƒ½ï¼Œæ— æ³•åœ¨è¡¨è¾¾ç±»å‹å†…éƒ¨ä¸å¤–éƒ¨
çš„å…³ç³»æ—¶ï¼Œç²¾ç¡®æ§åˆ¶å±æ€§é—´çš„è¿çº¿ã€‚
Mermaid å‚è€ƒæ‰‹å†Œï¼šlink:https://vscode.dev/github/mermaid-js/mermaid[Class diagrams]

UML ç®­å¤´ç¬¦å·åŠç±»å‹å…³ç³»çš„è¡¨è¾¾ï¼š

    classDiagram
    classA   --|> classB : Inheritance
    classC   --*  classD : Composition
    classE   --o  classF : Aggregation
    classG   -->  classH : Association
    classI   --   classJ : Link(Solid)
    classK   ..>  classL : Dependency
    classM   ..|> classN : Realization
    classO   ..   classP : Link(Dashed)
*****

ASG schema æè¿°çš„ AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£æ¡†æ¶ç»“æ„ç¤ºæ„å›¾å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š

[mermaid,target="mermaid-graph"]
--------------------------------
---
config:
  look: handDrawn
  theme: neutral
  layout: elk
---
classDiagram
    Document -- sectionBody
    Document -- author
    Document -- blockMetadata
    sectionBody -- section
    sectionBody -- blocks
    Document          <|-- inlines
    leafBlock         <|-- inlines
    dlistItem         <|-- inlines
    abstractListItem  <|-- inlines
    abstractBlock     <|-- inlines
    section             -- abstractHeading
    discreteHeading     -- abstractHeading
    abstractBlock <|-- abstractHeading
    abstractBlock <|-- abstractListItem
    abstractListItem <|-- listItem
    abstractListItem <|-- dlistItem
    abstractParentInline  <|-- inlineSpan 
    abstractParentInline  <|-- inlineRef 
    abstractParentInline  *-- inlines
    abstractParentInline  *-- location
    parentBlock     -- nonSectionBlockBody
    list            -- nonSectionBlockBody
    dlist           -- nonSectionBlockBody
    abstractBlock <|-- list
    abstractBlock <|-- dlist
    abstractBlock <|-- discreteHeading
    abstractBlock <|-- break
    abstractBlock <|-- blockMacro
    abstractBlock <|-- leafBlock
    abstractBlock <|-- parentBlock
    nonSectionBlockBody -- block
    nonSectionBlockBody -- abstractHeading
    blocks        *-- block
    block         *-- list
    block         *-- dlist
    block         *-- discreteHeading
    block         *-- break
    block         *-- blockMacro
    block         *-- leafBlock
    block         *-- parentBlock
    list          *-- listItem
    dlist         *-- dlistItem
    inlines       *-- inline
    inline        *-- inlineLiteral
    inline        *-- inlineRef
    inline        *-- inlineSpan
    location      *-- locationBoundary

    class author {
        address: string
        firstname: string
        fullname: string
        initials: string
        lastname: string
        middlename: strin
    }

    class blockMetadata {
        attributes: object
        location: location
        options: string[]
        roles: string[]
    }

    class Document {
        + attributes: object
        + blocks: sectionBody[block,section]
        + header: object
        + location: location
        + name: string
        + type: string
    }

    class abstractBlock{
        + id: string
        + location: location
        + metadata: blockMetadata
        + reftext: inlines
        + title: inlines
        + type: const(block)
    }

    class abstractHeading {
        level: intege
    }

    class abstractListItem {
        blocks: nonSectionBlockBody
        marker: string
        principal: inline
    }

    class abstractParentInline {
        inlines: inlines
        location: location
        type: const(inline)
    }

    class list {
        items: listItem[]
        marker: string
        name: const(list)
        variant: enum(callout, ordered, unordere)
    }

    class listItem {
        name: const(listItem)
    }

    class dlist {
        items: dlistItem[]
        marker: string
        name: const(dlist)
    }

    class dlistItem {
        name: const(dlistItem)
        terms: inlines[
    }

    class blockMacro {
        form: const(macro)
        name: enum(audio, video, image, toc)
        target: strin
    }

    class leafBlock {
        form: enum(delimited, indented, paragraph)
        inlines: inlines
        name: enum(listing, literal, paragraph, pass, stem, vers)
    }

    class parentBlock{
        + blocks: nonSectionBlockBody
        + delimiter: string
        + form: const(delimited)
        + name: enum(admonition, example, sidebar, open, quote)
    }

    class section {
        blocks: sectionBody
        name: const(section)
    }

    class break {
        name: const(break)
        variant: enum(page, themati)
    }

    class discreteHeading {
        name: const(heading)
    }


    class inlineLiteral {
        location: location
        name: enum(text, charref, raw)
        type: const(string)
        value: strin
    }

    class inlineRef {
        name: const(ref)
        target: string
        variant: enum(link, xre)
    }

    class inlineSpan {
        form: enum(constrained, unconstrained)
        name: const(span)
        variant: enum(strong, emphasis, code, mar)
    }

    class locationBoundary {
        col: integer
        file: string[]
        line: intege
    }
--------------------------------


ä»¥ä¸‹ä½¿ç”¨ jq è„šæœ¬å°† AsciiDoc ä¸­çš„æ–‡æ¡£å¯¹è±¡çš„å±æ€§æå–å‡ºæ¥ï¼š

[source,bash]
-------------
jq '. as $doc|keys|map(
  if . == "$defs" then 
    empty 
  elif . == "properties" then
    .={(.):$doc.[.]|keys|map(
      if $doc.properties.[.].["$ref"] then
        {(.):$doc.properties.[.].["$ref"]}
      else
        {(.):($doc.properties.[.].type?)}
      end
    )}
  else
    .={(.|tostring):($doc.[.].type? // $doc.[.])} 
  end
  ) | add | delpaths([["if"],["then"],["required"]])' /pl/asciidoc-lang/asg/schema.json |
  jq '.properties|add' | mlr --ijson --opprint --barred cat

+------------+---------------------+--------+------------------+--------+--------+
| attributes | blocks              | header | location         | name   | type   |
+------------+---------------------+--------+------------------+--------+--------+
| object     | #/$defs/sectionBody | object | #/$defs/location | string | string |
+------------+---------------------+--------+------------------+--------+--------+
-------------

å‘½ä»¤è¡Œä¸²è”äº†ä¸¤ä¸ª jq å‘½ä»¤ï¼Œå‰ä¸€ä¸ªç”¨äºæå– Document å¯¹è±¡çš„å„ç§å±æ€§ï¼Œç¬¬äºŒä¸ªç”¨äºæå– properties
å±æ€§åˆ—è¡¨ï¼Œç„¶åå†ä½¿ç”¨ Miller (mlr) å‘½ä»¤å°†é”®å€¼å¯¹è½¬æ¢ä¸ºè¡¨æ ¼å½¢å¼æ˜¾ç¤ºã€‚

  "$id": "https://schemas.asciidoc.org/asg/1-0-0/draft-01",
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "defaults": {
    "blocks": []
  },
  "description": "A structured representation of the semantics in an AsciiDoc document, primarily used for validating the compliance of an AsciiDoc processor.",
  "properties": [
    { "attributes": "object" },
    { "blocks": "#/$defs/sectionBody" },
    { "header": "object" },
    { "location": "#/$defs/location" },
    { "name": "string" },
    { "type": "string" }
  ],
  "title": "AsciiDoc Abstract Semantic Graph (ASG)",
  "type": "object"
}

å°†ç±»å‹åç§°åˆ—è¡¨ï¼ˆkeysï¼‰ä¸­é¡¹ä¸å…¶æœ¬èº«çš„æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ä¿¡æ¯å…³è”èµ·æ¥ã€‚ä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯å°† AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£èŠ‚ç‚¹ç±»å‹ä¸è„šæœ¬
è¯­è¨€å®ç°ä¸­çš„ç±»å‹å…³è”ã€‚å¯ä»¥çœ‹åˆ°ï¼Œé™¤äº† inlinesã€locationã€nonSectionBlockBodyã€sectionBody
ç­‰å››é¡¹ä¸ºæ•°ç»„ï¼ˆè®°å½•æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­å…¶å®ƒç±»å‹çš„ä¸€ä¸ªé›†åˆï¼‰ï¼Œå…¶ä½™ 22 é¡¹éƒ½æ˜¯ AsciiDoc çš„æ–‡æ¡£èŠ‚ç‚¹ç±»å‹ã€‚è€Œå…¶ä¸­çš„
å››ä¸ªæŠ½è±¡èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œæ˜¯å…¶å®ƒèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„åŸºç±»å®šä¹‰ã€‚Document ç±»å‹å®šä¹‰ä¸­ï¼Œå®šä¹‰äº† `blocks` å±æ€§ï¼ˆé›†åˆï¼‰
æ¥è®°å½•ç”¨æˆ·åœ¨æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­ç¼–å†™çš„å„ç§å—å¯¹è±¡ï¼ˆ`sectionBody`ï¼‰ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªé›†åˆåŒ…å« `block` æˆ–è€… `section`

[source,json]

  "section": "object",

  "inlines": "array",
  "location": "array",
  "nonSectionBlockBody": "array",
  "sectionBody": "array"

ç¬¼ç»Ÿåœ°è¯´ï¼ŒAsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­çš„å¯¹è±¡åŒ…å« `inline` å’Œ `block` ä¸¤ç±»å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œåˆ†ç±»å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼Œåé¢ä¸å†ç½—åˆ—ï¼š

* inline ("object") is neOf:
  ** "#/$defs/inlineSpan"
  ** "#/$defs/inlineRef"
  ** "#/$defs/inlineLiteral

* block ("object") is oneOf:
  ** "#/$defs/list"
  ** "#/$defs/dlist"
  ** "#/$defs/discreteHeading"
  ** "#/$defs/break"
  ** "#/$defs/blockMacro"
  ** "#/$defs/leafBlock"
  ** "#/$defs/parentBlock

è¿™é‡ŒæŒ‘é€‰ `parentBlock` è¿™ä¸ªæ¯”è¾ƒæœ‰ä»£è¡¨æ€§æ–‡æ¡£å¯¹è±¡æ¥è¯´æ˜ ASG æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­çš„ç±»å‹å…³ç³»ã€‚å…¶ä¸­ `$defs` è¡¨ç¤º
AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£å¯¹è±¡çš„å®šä¹‰åˆ—è¡¨ã€‚åˆ—è¡¨ä¸­çš„æ¯ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡ä¸­çš„ `type` è¡¨ç¤ºè¿™å¯¹è±¡ç±»å‹ï¼Œå¤šæ•°å¯¹è±¡éƒ½æ˜¯ AsciiDoc
æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­ç›´æ¥ä½¿ç”¨çš„ blocks æˆ–è€… inlines å¯¹è±¡ã€‚å…¶ä¸­ `required` æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªåˆ—è¡¨ï¼Œè¡¨ç¤ºå½“å‰å¯¹è±¡çš„å¿…è¦å±æ€§ã€‚
ASG æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­è¿˜å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ `if` æ¡ä»¶è¯­å¥ä¸€æ ·çš„åŠŸèƒ½ï¼Œç”¨æ¥åœ¨ç‰¹å®šæ¡ä»¶ä¸‹ä½¿ç”¨å½“å‰å¯¹è±¡çš„å±æ€§å‘ç”Ÿå˜åŒ–ã€‚å°±å¦‚ä»¥ä¸‹
ç‰‡æ®µä¸­ï¼Œå¦‚æœ `parentBlock` çš„åç§°çš„å€¼æ»¡è¶³ `admonition` è¿™ä¸ªå€¼ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆä¼šæˆä¸ºä¸€ä¸ªä¿¡æ¯æ¨¡å‹å¯¹è±¡ã€‚
AsciiDoc å…±æœ‰ 5 ç§ä¿¡æ¯æ¡†ï¼Œå¦‚å…¶ä¸­çš„ `variant` â€œå˜ä½“å±æ€§â€åˆ—è¡¨æ‰€ç¤ºã€‚å…¶ä¸­ `allOf` è¡¨ç¤ºå½“å‰å¯¹è±¡
çš„çˆ¶ç±»å‹ï¼Œè¿™é‡Œå°±è¡¨ç¤º `abstractBlock` æ˜¯çˆ¶ç±»å‹ï¼Œäº‹å®ä¸Šå®ƒæ˜¯å¤§å¤šæ•° AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£å¯¹è±¡çš„çˆ¶ç±»å‹ã€‚
ç„¶åå°±æ˜¯ `properties` å±æ€§åˆ—è¡¨ï¼Œå¯¹äºç”¨æˆ·æ¥è¯´ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªåˆ—è¡¨æ˜¯æœ€é‡è¦çš„ï¼Œå› ä¸ºæ¶‰åŠç”¨æˆ·å¦‚ä½•ç»™æ–‡æ¡£å¯¹è±¡
è®¾ç½®å„ç§å±æ€§ã€‚å½“ç„¶ï¼Œ`parentBlock` å¹¶ä¸”ä¸æ˜¯ç”¨æˆ·å¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥è®¾ç½®çš„ AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå®ƒæœ¬èº«å±æ€§
è§£æç¨‹åºç®¡ç†æ–‡æ¡£å¯¹è±¡çš„æ•°æ®ç»“æ„ï¼Œåªæœ‰åƒ "admonition", "example", "sidebar", "open", "quote"
æ‰æ˜¯ç”¨æˆ·ä½¿ç”¨ AsciiDoc å†™ä½œæ—¶åº”è¯¥å…³æ³¨çš„å…·ä½“çš„æ–‡æ¡£å¯¹è±¡ã€‚

[source,json]
-------------
        "parentBlock": {
          "type": "object",
          "allOf": [
            { "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractBlock" },
            {
              "if": {
                "required": ["name"],
                "properties": { "name": { "const": "admonition" } }
              },
              "then": {
                "required": ["variant"],
                "properties": {
                  "variant": {
                    "type": "string",
                    "enum": ["caution", "important", "note", "tip", "warning"]
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          ],
          "unevaluatedProperties": false,
          "required": ["name", "form", "delimiter"],
          "defaults": { "blocks": [] },
          "properties": {
            "name": {
              "type": "string",
              "enum": ["admonition", "example", "sidebar", "open", "quote"]
            },
            "form": { "type": "string", "const": "delimited" },
            "delimiter": { "type": "string" },
            "blocks": { "$ref": "#/$defs/nonSectionBlockBody" }
          }
        },
-------------

ä»¥ä¸‹ jq è„šæœ¬ç”¨äºæŠ½å– AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£å„ç§å¯¹è±¡çš„åç§°åŠå±æ€§åˆ—è¡¨ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬å®ƒä»¬çš„ç±»å‹å…³ç³»ã€‚è„šæœ¬åˆ†ä¸ºä¸¤éƒ¨åˆ†ï¼Œ
å‰é¢ `itemTypes` è¿™æ˜¯ç”¨äºè®°å½•å¯¹è±¡ç±»å‹çš„é›†åˆï¼Œå¯¹äºå…·ä½“çš„æŸç§ç±»å‹æ‰ä¼šæœ‰ `properties` å±æ€§åˆ—è¡¨ã€‚
è„šæœ¬ä¸­ä½¿ç”¨äº† `empty` å†…ç½®å‡½æ•°ï¼Œåªéœ€è¦ä½¿ç”¨ # ç¬¦å·å°†åŒ…å« empty çš„æ¡ä»¶å¥ä»¥åŠ itemTypes è¿™æ®µæ³¨è§£æ‰ï¼Œ
å°±å¯ä»¥è¾“å‡ºè¿™äº›å…·ä½“ç±»å‹çš„å±æ€§åˆ—è¡¨ã€‚

[source,bash]
-------------
jq  '.["$defs"] as $defs|$defs|keys|map(
  {(.):{
    type: ($defs.[.].type | if .== "array" then empty else . end),
    # itemTypes: (
    #   if($defs.[.].type == "array") then 
    #   [ $defs.[.] |
    #     if (.prefixItems) then
    #       .prefixItems[] | map(.|gsub("#/\\$defs/"; "")) | add
    #     elif (.items.oneOf) then
    #       .items.oneOf[] | map(.|gsub("#/\\$defs/"; "")) | add
    #     elif (.items) then
    #       .items         | map(.|gsub("#/\\$defs/"; ""))  | add
    #     else
    #       .|tostring
    #     end
    #   ] else empty end),
    properties: ($defs.[.].properties as $pp | $pp // {}|keys?|map(
      if ($pp.[.].["$ref"]) then
        (.+$pp.[.].["$ref"]) | gsub("#/\\$defs/"; ": ")
      elif ($pp.[.].type == "array") then
        if ($pp.[.].items.["$ref"]) then
          (.+$pp.[.].items.["$ref"] | gsub("#/\\$defs/"; ": ")+"[]")
        else
          (.+": "+$pp.[.].items.type+"[]")
        end
      elif ($pp.[.].enum) then
        (.+": enum{"+($pp.[.].enum|join(", "))+"}")
      elif ($pp.[.].const) then
        (.+": const("+$pp.[.].const+")")
      else
        (.+": "+$pp.[.].type)
      end
      ))
    }
  })
  ' /pl/asciidoc-lang/asg/schema.json
-------------

  {
    "inlines": {
      "type": "array",
      "itemTypes": [ "inline" ]
    }
  },
  {
    "location": {
      "type": "array",
      "itemTypes": [ "locationBoundary", "locationBoundary" ]
    }
  },
  {
    "nonSectionBlockBody": {
      "type": "array",
      "itemTypes": [ "block" ]
    }
  },
  {
    "sectionBody": {
      "type": "array",
      "itemTypes": [ "block", "section" ]
    }
  }
]

[
  {
    "abstractBlock": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "id: string",
        "location: location",
        "metadata: blockMetadata",
        "reftext: inlines",
        "title: inlines",
        "type: const(block)"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "abstractHeading": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "level: integer"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "abstractListItem": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "blocks: nonSectionBlockBody",
        "marker: string",
        "principal: inlines"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "abstractParentInline": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "inlines: inlines",
        "location: location",
        "type: const(inline)"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "author": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "address: string",
        "firstname: string",
        "fullname: string",
        "initials: string",
        "lastname: string",
        "middlename: string"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "blockMacro": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "form: const(macro)",
        "name: enum{audio, video, image, toc}",
        "target: string"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "blockMetadata": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "attributes: object",
        "location: location",
        "options: string[]",
        "roles: string[]"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "break": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "name: const(break)",
        "variant: enum{page, thematic}"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "discreteHeading": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "name: const(heading)"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "dlist": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "items: dlistItem[]",
        "marker: string",
        "name: const(dlist)"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "dlistItem": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "name: const(dlistItem)",
        "terms: inlines[]"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "inlineLiteral": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "location: location",
        "name: enum{text, charref, raw}",
        "type: const(string)",
        "value: string"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "inlineRef": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "name: const(ref)",
        "target: string",
        "variant: enum{link, xref}"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "inlineSpan": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "form: enum{constrained, unconstrained}",
        "name: const(span)",
        "variant: enum{strong, emphasis, code, mark}"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "leafBlock": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "form: enum{delimited, indented, paragraph}",
        "inlines: inlines",
        "name: enum{listing, literal, paragraph, pass, stem, verse}"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "list": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "items: listItem[]",
        "marker: string",
        "name: const(list)",
        "variant: enum{callout, ordered, unordered}"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "listItem": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "name: const(listItem)"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "locationBoundary": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "col: integer",
        "file: string[]",
        "line: integer"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "parentBlock": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "blocks: nonSectionBlockBody",
        "delimiter: string",
        "form: const(delimited)",
        "name: enum{admonition, example, sidebar, open, quote}"
      ]
    }
  },
  {
    "section": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": [
        "blocks: sectionBody",
        "name: const(section)"
      ]
    }

.AsciiDoc link:{schema_json}[ASG schema.json].
:schema_json: https://gitlab.eclipse.org/eclipse/asciidoc-lang/asciidoc-lang/-/blob/main/asg/schema.json
[source,json]

{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://schemas.asciidoc.org/asg/1-0-0/draft-01",
  "title": "AsciiDoc Abstract Semantic Graph (ASG)",
  "description": "A structured representation of the semantics in an AsciiDoc document, primarily used for validating the compliance of an AsciiDoc processor.",
  "type": "object",
  "required": ["name", "type"],
  "defaults": { "blocks": [] },
  "additionalProperties": false,
  "properties": {
    "name": { "type": "string", "const": "document" },
    "type": { "type": "string", "const": "block" },
    "attributes": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "patternProperties": {
        "^[a-zA-Z0-9_][-a-zA-Z0-9_]*$": {
          "oneOf": [
            { "type": "string" },
            { "type": "null" }
          ]
        }
      }
    },
    "header": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "title": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlines" },
        "authors": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/author" },
          "minItems": 1
        },
        "location": { "$ref": "#/$defs/location" }
      }
    },
    "blocks": { "$ref": "#/$defs/sectionBody" },
    "location": { "$ref": "#/$defs/location" }
  },
  "if": {
    "required": ["header"]
  },
  "then": {
    "required": ["attributes"]
  },
  "$defs": {
    "abstractBlock": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["type"],
      "properties": {
        "type": { "type": "string", "const": "block" },
        "id": { "type": "string" },
        "title": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlines" },
        "reftext": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlines" },
        "metadata": { "$ref": "#/$defs/blockMetadata" },
        "location": { "$ref": "#/$defs/location" }
      }
    },
    "abstractHeading": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractBlock" }],
      "required": ["title", "level"],
      "properties": {
        "level": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 0 }
      }
    },
    "abstractListItem": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractBlock" }],
      "required": ["marker"],
      "defaults": { "blocks": [] },
      "properties": {
        "marker": { "type": "string" },
        "principal": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlines" },
        "blocks": { "$ref": "#/$defs/nonSectionBlockBody" }
      }
    },
    "sectionBody": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": {
        "type": "object",
        "oneOf": [
          { "$ref": "#/$defs/block" },
          { "$ref": "#/$defs/section" }
        ]
      }
    },
    "nonSectionBlockBody": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/block" }
    },
    "section": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractHeading" }],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name"],
      "defaults": { "blocks": [] },
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "const": "section" },
        "blocks": { "$ref": "#/$defs/sectionBody" }
      }
    },
    "block": {
      "type": "object",
      "discriminator": { "propertyName": "name" },
      "oneOf": [
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/list" },
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/dlist" },
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/discreteHeading" },
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/break" },
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/blockMacro" },
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/leafBlock" },
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/parentBlock" }
      ]
    },
    "list": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractBlock" }],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name", "marker", "variant", "items"],
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "const": "list" },
        "marker": { "type": "string" },
        "variant": { "type": "string", "enum": ["callout", "ordered", "unordered"] },
        "items": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/listItem" },
          "minItems": 1
        }
      }
    },
    "dlist": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractBlock" }],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name", "marker", "items"],
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "const": "dlist" },
        "marker": { "type": "string" },
        "items": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/dlistItem" },
          "minItems": 1
        }
      }
    },
    "listItem": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractListItem" }],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name", "principal"],
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "const": "listItem" }
      }
    },
    "dlistItem": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractListItem" }],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name", "terms"],
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "const": "dlistItem" },
        "terms": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlines" },
          "minItems": 1
        }
      }
    },
    "discreteHeading": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractHeading" }],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name"],
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "const": "heading" }
      }
    },
    "break": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractBlock" }],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name", "variant"],
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "const": "break" },
        "variant": { "type": "string", "enum": ["page", "thematic"] }
      }
    },
    "blockMacro": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractBlock" }],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name", "form"],
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "enum": ["audio", "video", "image", "toc"] },
        "form": { "type": "string", "const": "macro" },
        "target": { "type": "string" }
      }
    },
    "leafBlock": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractBlock" },
        {
          "if": {
            "required": ["form"],
            "properties": { "form": { "const": "delimited" } }
          },
          "then": {
            "required": ["delimiter"],
            "properties": { "delimiter": { "type": "string" }
            }
          }
        }
      ],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name"],
      "defaults": { "inlines": [] },
      "properties": {
        "name": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["listing", "literal", "paragraph", "pass", "stem", "verse"]
        },
        "form": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["delimited", "indented", "paragraph"]
        },
        "inlines": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlines" }
      }
    },
    "parentBlock": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractBlock" },
        {
          "if": {
            "required": ["name"],
            "properties": { "name": { "const": "admonition" } }
          },
          "then": {
            "required": ["variant"],
            "properties": {
              "variant": {
                "type": "string",
                "enum": ["caution", "important", "note", "tip", "warning"]
              }
            }
          }
        }
      ],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name", "form", "delimiter"],
      "defaults": { "blocks": [] },
      "properties": {
        "name": {
          "type": "string",
          "enum": ["admonition", "example", "sidebar", "open", "quote"]
        },
        "form": { "type": "string", "const": "delimited" },
        "delimiter": { "type": "string" },
        "blocks": { "$ref": "#/$defs/nonSectionBlockBody" }
      }
    },
    "blockMetadata": {
      "type": "object",
      "defaults": { "attributes": {}, "options": [], "roles": [] },
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "attributes": {
          "type": "object",
          "additionalProperties": false,
          "patternProperties": {
            "^(?:[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_-]*|\\$[1-9][0-9]*)$": {
              "type": "string"
            }
          }
        },
        "options": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": { "type": "string" }
        },
        "roles": {
          "type": "array",
          "items": { "type": "string" }
        },
        "location": { "$ref": "#/$defs/location" }
      }
    },
    "inlines": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inline" }
    },
    "inline": {
      "type": "object",
      "discriminator": { "propertyName": "name" },
      "oneOf": [
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlineSpan" },
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlineRef" },
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlineLiteral" }
      ]
    },
    "abstractParentInline": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["type", "inlines"],
      "properties": {
        "type": { "type": "string", "const": "inline" },
        "inlines": { "$ref": "#/$defs/inlines" },
        "location": { "$ref": "#/$defs/location" }
      }
    },
    "inlineSpan": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractParentInline" }],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name", "variant", "form"],
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "const": "span" },
        "variant": { "type": "string", "enum": ["strong", "emphasis", "code", "mark"] },
        "form": { "type": "string", "enum": ["constrained", "unconstrained"] }
      }
    },
    "inlineRef": {
      "type": "object",
      "allOf": [{ "$ref": "#/$defs/abstractParentInline" }],
      "unevaluatedProperties": false,
      "required": ["name", "variant", "target"],
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "const": "ref" },
        "variant": { "type": "string", "enum": ["link", "xref"] },
        "target": { "type": "string" }
      }
    },
    "inlineLiteral": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["name", "type", "value"],
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "name": { "type": "string", "enum": ["text", "charref", "raw"] },
        "type": { "type": "string", "const": "string" },
        "value": { "type": "string" },
        "location": { "$ref": "#/$defs/location" }
      }
    },
    "author": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": false,
      "properties": {
        "fullname": { "type": "string" },
        "initials": { "type": "string" },
        "firstname": { "type": "string" },
        "middlename": { "type": "string" },
        "lastname": { "type": "string" },
        "address": { "type": "string" }
      }

    "location": {
      "type": "array",
      "prefixItems": [
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/locationBoundary" },
        { "$ref": "#/$defs/locationBoundary" }
      ],
      "minItems": 2,
      "maxItems": 2
    },
    "locationBoundary": {
      "type": "object",

[[blocks]]
== Blocks

AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸»è¦æ˜¯å—å…ƒç´ ï¼ˆBlockï¼‰å’Œå†…è”å…ƒç´ ï¼ˆInlineï¼‰ï¼Œåè€…ä¸»è¦æ˜¯æ­£æ–‡æ®µè½å†…å®¹ï¼Œ
å‰è€…åˆ™æœ‰å„ç§ä¸åŒç”¨é€”çš„å—å…ƒç´ ã€‚å½“ç„¶ï¼Œå—å…ƒç´ å†…ä¹ŸåŒ…å«äº†å†…è”å…ƒç´ ã€‚

AsciiDoc Language Specification Outline å®˜æ–¹è§„èŒƒå¤§çº²æ–‡æ¡£åŒ…å«äº†éå¸¸ä¸°å¯Œçš„è½¯ä»¶è®¾è®¡ç»†èŠ‚ã€‚
åœ¨è¯­è¨€è§„èŒƒå¤§çº²æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­ Blocks ä¸€ç« å†…å®¹ç½—åˆ—è®²è§£äº†å„ç§å—å…ƒç´ ã€‚å…¶ä¸­ï¼Œåˆ—è¡¨æ˜¯ä¸ç”¨åˆ†ç•Œç¬¦å·é™å®šå†…å®¹
èŒƒå›´çš„å—å…ƒç´ ï¼Œå®ƒçš„å®šä¹‰ç¬¦å· (List markers) åŒ…æ‹¬ï¼š

.  `+*+` (asterisk, unordered), 
.  `.` (period, ordered), 
.  `[1-9][0-9]*.` (Arabic number, ordered), 
.  `-` (hyphen, unordered), and 
.  `<([1-9][0-9]*|\.)>` (callout)

Callout ç¼–å·ç”¨äºåœ¨ä»£ç å—ä¸­ç»™ `<.>` æ‰€åœ¨çš„ç›¸åº”ä½ç½®äº§ç”Ÿä¸€ä¸ªç¼–ç ï¼Œä¸»è¦ç”¨äºè§£é‡Šä»£ç ç”¨ã€‚
Callout ç¼–å·éœ€è¦æˆå¯¹ä½¿ç”¨ï¼Œæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ª `<.>` æ ‡è®°åœ¨ä»£ç ä¸­ï¼Œå°±éœ€è¦åŒæ ·æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªåœ¨ä»£ç å—åé¢ã€‚
è¿™äº›ç¼–å·è¿˜å¯ä»¥ä¸ `icons=font` æ–‡æ¡£å±æ€§æ­é…ä½¿ç”¨ï¼Œæ˜¾ç¤ºä¸åŒçš„åºå·å›¾æ¡ˆã€‚å¯¹äºæœ‰ç›¸åŒçš„ç¼–å·ï¼Œ
è¿˜å¯ä»¥è®¾ç½®æŒ‡å®šçš„ç¼–å·ï¼Œä¾‹å¦‚ `<1>`ï¼Œå‚è€ƒä»¥ä¸‹ä»£ç å—ï¼š

.Examples of Ordered or Unordered List.
------
.   Ordered list item with auto increment numbers.
1.  Ordered list item with Arabic numerals.
a.  Lowrcase alphabet order List item.
F.  Uppercase alphabet order List item.
i)  Lowercase Roman numeric list item.
I)  Uppercase Roman numeric list item.

[] <.>
- Unordered List item.
* Unordered List item.
** Unordered List item.
*** Unordered List item.

[] <.>
* [*] checked
* [x] also checked
* [ ] not checked
*     normal list item

Description list:: Also named Dlist as a abbreviation.
Depth::: More depeth by a diferent Dlist markers.
------
<.> Breaks the ordered list above.
<.> Breaks the unordered list above.

æ–‡å­—å†…å®¹ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨å†…ç½®çš„ `{empty}` ç©ºå­—ç¬¦æ›¿æ¢æŒ‡ä»¤ç»“åˆ Description lists æŒ‡ä»¤ `::` è¿›è¡Œ
ç¼©è¿›å¤„ç†ï¼Œè¿˜å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨`:::` è¿›è¡ŒäºŒçº§ç¼©è¿›ã€‚åªè¦é¦–å…ˆä¸è¿›è¡Œç¼©è¿›ï¼ŒåŒä¸€æ®µè½ä¸­çš„å…¶å®ƒåç»­å†…å®¹å¯ä»¥ä»»æ„

*  block å½¢å¼çš„å›¾ç‰‡å®ï¼š`+image::play.png[]+`
*  inline å½¢å¼çš„å›¾ç‰‡å®ï¼š`+image:play.png[]+`

AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£å—åŒ…å«çš„å†…å®¹ç±»å‹æŒ‰ä»¥ä¸‹åˆ†ç±»ï¼š

.Content model
[cols="^1,5"]
|=============
|compound  |a block that may only contain other blocks (e.g., a section)
|simple    |a block that's treated as contiguous lines of paragraph text 
            (and subject to normal substitutions) (e.g., a paragraph block)
|verbatim  |a block that holds verbatim text (displayed "`as is`") 
            (and subject to verbatim substitutions) (e.g., a listing block)
|raw       |a block that holds unprocessed content passed directly through
            to the output with no substitutions applied 
            (e.g., a passthrough block)
|empty     |a block that has no content (e.g., an image block)
|table     |a special content model reserved for tables that enforces 
            a fixed structure
|=============


.Built-in contexts
[#table-of-contexts,cols="1s,5"]
|===
|Name           | Purpose

|admonition     |One of five admonition blocks.
|audio          |An audio block.
|colist         |A callout list.
|dlist          |A description list.
|document       |The top-level document or the document in an AsciiDoc table cell
|example        |An example block.
|floating_title |A discrete heading.
|image          |An image block.
|list_item      |An item in an ordered, unordered, or description list 
                 (only relevant inside a list or description list block).
                 In a description list, this block is used to represent 
                 the term and the description.
|listing        |A listing block.
|literal        |A literal block.
|olist          |An ordered list.
|open           |An open block.
|page_break     |A page break.
|paragraph      |A paragraph.
|pass           |A passthrough block.
|preamble       |The preamble of the document.
|quote          |A quote block (aka blockquote).
|section        |A section. May also be a part, chapter, or special section.
|sidebar        |A sidebar block.
|table          |A table block.
|table_cell     |A table cell (only relevant inside a table block).
|thematic_break |A thematic break (aka horizontal rule).
|toc            |A TOC block (to designate custom TOC placement).
|ulist          |An unordered list.
|verse          |A verse block.
|video          |A video block.
|===

è¿™äº›è‡ªåŠ¨ç¼–å·æŒ‡ä»¤åŒ…æ‹¬å¤šç§å†…å®¹ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ listing ç¼–å·å¯¹åº” [source] ä»£ç å—ï¼Œæ ‡é¢˜ç¼–å·åˆ™ä½¿ç”¨

:listing-number: 0
:listing-caption:

.Example of Block Title Numbering
[source,adoc]
-------------
  :sectnums!:
  == Preface

  :sectnums:
  == First Chapter

  :listing-caption!:
  :listing-caption:
  :listing-caption: My Listing
  :listing-number: H

  .Example Block Title
  ====
  content
  ====

  .Sidebar Block Title (Center)
  ****
  content
  ****

  [sidebar]
  single line sidebar block.

  .Listing Block Title
  -----
  content
  -----

  .Quote Block Title
  ____
  content
  ____

  [quote]
  single line quote block.
-------------

* ä½œä¸ºå†…å®¹ç›´é€šå¤„ç†ï¼ˆpass throughsï¼‰ï¼ŒåŒ…è£¹é‚£äº›éœ€è¦é¿å…è¢«å¤„ç†ç¨‹åºæ›¿æ¢çš„å†…å®¹ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å•åŠ å·ã€åŒåŠ å·ã€ä¸‰è¿æˆ–è€…ä»¥ä¸Šã€‚
* ä½œä¸ºåˆ—è¡¨ä¸­çš„æ®µè½è¿æ¥ç¬¦å·ï¼Œå› ä¸º AsciiDoc æ˜¯ç¼©è¿›æ•æ„Ÿçš„æ–‡æ¡£ï¼Œåœ¨åˆ—è¡¨ä¸­ç¼–å†™çš„å¤šä¸ªæ­£æ–‡æ®µè½ï¼Œå°±é€šè¿‡ç‹¬å ä¸€è¡Œçš„åŠ å·æ¥è¿æ¥ã€‚
* ä½œä¸ºå¼ºåˆ¶æ–­è¡Œï¼ˆhard line breakï¼‰ï¼Œåœ¨åŠ å·å‰ç¼€ç©ºæ ¼å¹¶æ”¾ç½®äºè¡Œæœ«ï¼Œå¯æœ‰åç¼€ç©ºæ ¼ã€‚
* ä¸å±æ€§å€¼ä¸­ä½¿ç”¨çš„è½¯ä»¶æ–­è¡Œ (`\`) ç¬¦å·ä¸€èµ·ä½¿ç”¨ï¼Œåœ¨å±æ€§å€¼çš„è½¯æ–­è¡Œä½ç½®ä½¿ç”¨ `+ \` ä»¥å®ç°ä¿ç•™ç¡¬æ–­è¡Œçš„å±æ€§å€¼å†…å®¹ã€‚

[TIP]
=====
åˆ—è¡¨ä¸­ä½¿ç”¨ `+` ç¬¦å·è¿æ¥å¤šä¸ªæ®µè½æˆ–ä»£ç å—æ—¶ï¼Œå¯ä»¥åœ¨å…¶å‰åä¿ç•™ç©ºè¡Œã€‚ä½†æ˜¯åœ¨ä½¿ç”¨å‰å¯¼ç©ºè¡Œæ—¶
ä¸èƒ½å¯¹ `+` ç¬¦å·è¿›è¡Œç¼©è¿›ï¼Œä¼šè¢«å½“ä½œæ–‡æœ¬å—å¤„ç†ã€‚å¯ä»¥è€ƒè™‘åœ¨è¡Œå‰ä½¿ç”¨ `{empty}` æˆ–è€… `{blank}`
ï¼ˆå±æ€§å¼•ç”¨ï¼‰ç©ºç™½å†…å®¹ä½œä¸ºæ–‡æœ¬ç¼©è¿›æ›¿ä»£å½¢å¼ã€‚ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯ç”¨ soft line break æ¥ç»™ä¸€æ®µå†…å®¹æ–­è¡Œï¼š

[source,asciidoc]
----
:CRLF: {empty} + \
  {empty}

UTF-8:: "unicode-1-1-utf-8" {CRLF} "unicode11utf8" {CRLF} "unicode20utf8"

æ–­è¡Œæ•ˆæœæ¼”ç¤ºå¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š

:CRLF: {empty} + \
  {empty}

UTF-8:: "unicode-1-1-utf-8" {CRLF} "unicode11utf8" {CRLF} "unicode20utf8" 
        {CRLF} "utf-8" {CRLF} "utf8" {CRLF} "x-unicode20utf8"
=====

ç”±äºï¼ŒåŠ å·åœ¨ AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£çš„åº”ç”¨éå¸¸é¢‘ç¹ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥é˜…è¯»å¹¶ç†è§£ AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­çš„å®å®šä¹‰ï¼Œç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå°±
åº”è¯¥æ˜¯ç†è§£ç›´é€šå®çš„ä½¿ç”¨ï¼Œæœ¬æ–‡å°†ç›´é€šå®çš„å†…å®¹ç‹¬ç«‹åœ¨ä¸€ç« è¿›è¡Œè§£è¯´ï¼Œåç»­å†…å®¹å°†ä»¥ <<substitution>>ã€
<<document_attributes>>ã€<<passthroughs>> çš„é¡ºåºç»„ç»‡ã€‚

æŒ‰ç…§è§„èŒƒæ–‡æ¡£æè¿°ï¼ŒAsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­çš„ç©ºç™½ç¬¦å·ï¼ˆSpace charactersï¼‰åŒ…æ‹¬ç©ºæ ¼ã€æ¢è¡Œç¬¦ã€åˆ¶è¡¨ç¬¦ï¼Œ
å®ƒä»¬åœ¨æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­çš„åŠŸèƒ½è¯´æ˜å¦‚ä¸‹ã€‚è§„èŒƒæ–‡æ¡£ä¸­çš„ *FI* è¡¨æœªæ¥è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜ï¼ˆFuture Issueï¼‰ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬è§„èŒƒçš„
ææ¡ˆã€è®¨è®ºã€æ¦‚å¿µæ¾„æ¸…ï¼š

* An AsciiDoc document may use tabs or spaces as space characters, though the 
  inline syntax primarily only considers spaces.
* A space character is a space, tab, or line ending (e.g., newline).
 ** *FI* Precisely, what space characters are permitted (e.g., space, tab, newline) 
    or restricted? (For example, `\s` includes no-break space (`\u00a0`) in JavaScript, 
    but not in Ruby.)
* Other space characters are permitted in the document, but will not be interpreted as such.
* Newlines create separate lines, which are often treated specially in AsciiDoc.
* Empty lines are often treated as significant when analyzing the block structure of an AsciiDoc document
* Two consecutive line endings create an empty line; consecutive empty lines in 
  non-verbatim content are semantically equivalent to a single empty line
* Except in verbatim or raw content or block metadata, an empty line is interpreted 
  as a block boundary.
* Leading space characters make an indented line.
* Trailing space characters are insignificant and may be dropped by the processor.
 ** *FI* How are trailing space characters in the source going to be handled?
* The one exception is a non-AsciiDoc include file with lines that include trailing space 
  characters; these characters must be preserved.


ä½¿ç”¨ä»¥ä¸‹ä»»ä¸€ç§æ–¹å¼å¯ä»¥å°†å†…å®¹è®¾ç½®ä¸ºå­—é¢é‡å—å¯¹è±¡ï¼ˆliteral blockï¼‰ï¼Œå’Œä»£ç å—ç±»ä¼¼ä¹Ÿä¼šåœ¨è½¬æ¢
HTML æ ¼å¼æ—¶ä½¿ç”¨ `<pre>` åŒ…è£¹å†…å®¹ï¼š

* indenting the first line of a paragraph by one or more spaces,
* setting the `literal` style on a block using an attribute list, or
* enclosing the content within a pair of literal block delimiters (`\....` ).

AsciiDoc é»˜è®¤ä¼šå°†ç¼©è¿›å½“ä½œä»£ç å—å†…å®¹ï¼ŒAsciiDoc ä¸­çš„ç¼©è¿›å½¢å¼ä¸»è¦åŒ…æ‹¬ï¼š

*   åˆ—è¡¨ç¼©è¿›ï¼šç”¨äºæ— åºåˆ—è¡¨ã€æœ‰åºåˆ—è¡¨ï¼Œä»¥åŠ Dlist æœ¯è¯­è¡¨è¿›è¡Œç¼©è¿›ã€‚
*   å—å¯¹è±¡å†…å®¹ç¼©è¿›ï¼šç”¨äºä»£ç å—å’Œè¡Œå†…ä»£ç ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬ä½¿ç”¨ `----` æˆ–è€… `====` ç­‰ç­‰åˆ†ç•Œç¬¦åŒ…è£¹çš„å†…å®¹ã€‚
*   è¡¨æ ¼ç¼©è¿›ï¼šç”¨äºå¯¹é½è¡¨æ ¼å†…å®¹ã€‚é™¤éå¯ç”¨å•å…ƒçš„è¯­æ³•æ”¯æŒï¼Œå¦åˆ™ç¼©è¿›å†…å®¹ä¸ä¼šå½“ä½œä»£ç å—çœ‹å¾…ã€‚
*   æ•°å­¦å…¬å¼ç¼©è¿›ï¼šä½¿ç”¨ `pass:[++++]` åˆ†ç•Œç¬¦åŒ…è£¹å—å…¬å¼å†…å®¹ï¼Œå…¶ç¼©è¿›ä¼šåŸæ · (passthrough) ä¼ é€’ç»™å…¬å¼è§£æå™¨ã€‚
*   æ³¨é‡Šç¼©è¿›ï¼šä½¿ç”¨ // ç”¨äºå•è¡Œå’Œä½¿ç”¨ /// å¤šè¡Œæ³¨é‡Šï¼Œç¼©è¿›åŸæ ·ä¿ç•™ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”ä¸ä¼šæ¸²æŸ“åˆ°è¾“å‡ºæ–‡ä»¶ã€‚

æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­ä¸ºäº†æ­£æ–‡æ®µè½çš„ç¼©è¿›å¯¹é½ï¼Œå¯ä»¥åœ¨é¦–è¡Œä½¿ç”¨é”šç‚¹ï¼ˆanchor poinï¼‰å¼€å¤´ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ `[[A]]` è¿™æ ·çš„æ ¼å¼ï¼Œ
ç„¶åå…¶å®ƒå†…å®¹ã€åŒ…æ‹¬åé¢è¿ç»­çš„è¡Œéƒ½å¯ä»¥ä»»æ„ç¼©è¿›ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”è¿™äº›è¡Œé¦–ã€è¡Œæœ«çš„ç©ºç™½ç¬¦å·ä¼šè¢«è¿‡æ»¤æ‰ã€‚
AsciiDoc å­—å¤„ç†ç¨‹åºï¼ˆPreprocessorï¼‰ä¼šåœ¨è¯»å–æ­£æ–‡å†…å®¹ï¼ˆparagraphï¼‰æ—¶è¿›è¡Œå½’ä¸€åŒ–å¤„ç†
ï¼ˆline normalizationï¼‰ï¼Œå»é™¤æ‰è¡Œæœ«çš„ç©ºç™½å­—ç¬¦ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬æ¢è¡Œç¬¦å·ã€‚è‡ªå®šä¹‰çš„æ–­è¡Œå¤„ç†éœ€è¦
æ ¹æ®ä»¥ä¸Šæ–¹æ³•æˆ–è€…ä½¿ç”¨å®ã€åˆ—è¡¨ã€ä»£ç å—ç­‰ç­‰æ–¹æ³•å¤„ç†ã€‚

è§„èŒƒæ–‡æ¡£ä¸­å…³äºå†…å®¹ç¼©è¿›ï¼ˆIndentationï¼‰çš„éƒ¨åˆ†è¯´æ˜ï¼š

*   AsciiDoc is a start margin-aligned (i.e., left-aligned in ltr) language.
*   Using the start margin as an anchor point in the syntax makes moving content 
    around easier, avoids the problem of excessive/compound indentation, encourages 
    the author to be more explicit about nesting, and makes the language easier to parse.
*   That means, with certain exceptions, space characters at the start of a line 
    (an indented line) are significant.
*   The key exception are list markers, which may be indented without meaning.
*   A line with leading space characters at a block boundary makes a literal paragraph.
*   Spaces are recommended for indentation, but tabs may also be used.

[reftext="å†…å®¹æ›¿æ¢"]
[[substitution]]
== Substitution


AsciiDoc æœ‰ 6 ç§å†…å®¹æ›¿æ¢å½¢å¼ï¼Œç›¸å…³æ–‡æ¡£è¯´æ˜å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š

.Substitution types
[cols="1,2,2"]
|====
| Substitutions     | Examples                    | subs/pages/index.adoc

| Specialchars      | i.e < (wil be `\&lt;`)      | special-characters.adoc
| Quotes            | i.e., inline formatting     | quotes.adoc
| Attributes        | \{docname}: {docname}       | attributes.adoc
| Replacements      | i.e. +(C)+ is copyright (C) | replacements.adoc
| Macros            | i.e. `\pass:a[\{docname}]`  | macros.adoc
| Post replacements | one case is line break (+)  | post-replacements.adoc
|====

å…¶ä¸­åç½®æ›¿æ¢ï¼ˆPost Replacement Substitutionsï¼‰æ˜¯åœ¨å…¶å®ƒæ›¿æ¢å®Œæˆåè¿›è¡Œçš„æœ€åä¸€æ­¥æ›¿æ¢ã€‚
ä¸»è¦æ˜¯æ–­è¡Œç¬¦å·ï¼ˆline break character, `{plus}`)ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªç¬¦å·ç”¨åœ¨è¡Œæœªç»“æŸä»¥ä¿ç•™æ¢è¡Œç¬¦å·ï¼Œ
ç›¸å½“äº HTML ä¸­çš„ `<br>` æ–­è¡Œã€‚åœ¨å­—ç¬¦å¤„ç†å™¨æ‰§è¡Œ `post_replacements` æ­¥éª¤æ—¶æ›¿æ¢ã€‚
Markdown å’Œ reStructuredText æ ¼å¼ä¸­åˆ†åˆ«ä½¿ç”¨ç»“å°¾çš„ \ å’Œå‰å¯¼çš„ | ç¬¦å·è¡¨ç¤ºæ–­è¡Œã€‚
Markdown è¿˜å¯ä»¥åœ¨è¡Œæœ«ä½¿ç”¨ 2 ä¸ªç©ºæ ¼è¡¨ç¤ºä¿ç•™æ¢è¡Œã€‚

å®æ›¿æ¢æ­¥éª¤ï¼ˆMacro Substitutionsï¼‰åœ¨å­—ç¬¦æ›¿æ¢ï¼ˆCharacter Replacement Substitutionsï¼‰
æ­¥éª¤å®Œæˆåè¿›è¡Œï¼Œæ‰€æœ‰ä¸å®ç›¸å…³çš„å†…å®¹æ›¿æ¢éƒ½åœ¨è¿™ä¸ªæ­¥éª¤è¿›è¡Œï¼Œinline æˆ–è€… block å®ã€‚ç”¨æˆ·å¯ä»¥
å¯¹å®è¿›è¡Œé…ç½®ï¼Œä»¥å½±å“å†…å®¹æ›¿æ¢è¡Œä¸ºã€‚è¿™ä¹Ÿæ˜¯ä¸»è¦çš„ AsciiDoc å†…å®¹å¤„ç†æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œä¸»è¦æœ‰ä¸¤ç§é…ç½®å½¢å¼ï¼š

* é€šè¿‡ `sups` å±æ€§é…ç½® block å†…å®¹çš„æ›¿æ¢è§„åˆ™ï¼Œå‚è€ƒï¼šapply-subs-to-blocks.adocï¼›
* é€šè¿‡ç¼©å†™å½¢å¼é…ç½® inline pass macro (`++pass:[]++`)ï¼Œå‚è€ƒï¼šapply-subs-to-text.adoc ï¼›

ç‰¹æ®Šå­—ç¬¦æ˜¯æŒ‡ HTML ä¸­çš„æ ‡ç­¾èµ·æ­¢ç¬¦å·ç­‰ç­‰ï¼Œä¼šè¢«æ›¿æ¢ä¸º named character reference ï¼š
å°äºå·å’Œå¤§äºå·ï¼ˆ`<`ï¼Œ`>`ï¼‰åˆ†åˆ«æ›¿æ¢ä¸º `\&lt;` `\&gt;`ï¼Œä¸å·ï¼ˆampersandï¼‰`&` æ›¿æ¢ä¸º `\&amp;`ã€‚
ä»¥ä¸‹è¡¨æ ¼æ˜¾ç¤ºäº† AsciiDoc å…ƒç´ ä¸­é»˜è®¤çš„ç‰¹æ®Šå­—ç¬¦æ›¿æ¢è§„åˆ™ï¼Œç›´é€šå†…å®¹å’Œæ³¨è§£ä¸æ›¿æ¢ç‰¹æ®Šå­—ç¬¦ã€‚
å¹¶ä¸”ï¼Œç‰¹æ®Šå­—ç¬¦æ›¿æ¢æ­¥éª¤ï¼ˆstepï¼‰ç­‰äºå±æ€§å€¼æ›¿æ¢ï¼ˆattribute substitutionï¼‰ï¼Œé¡ºåºå‚è€ƒä¸Šè¡¨ã€‚

.Blocks and inline elements subject to the substitution step applied by default
[#table-substitution,cols="~,^,^,^,^,^,^"]
:y: pass:q[#YES#]
:n: No
:DSS: Special characters substitution
:DQS: Default quotes substitution
:DAS: Default attributes substitution
:CRS: Character Replacement Substitutions
:MS:  Macro Substitutions
:PRS: Post Replacement Substitutions
|=====================================
|Blocks and elements           |{DSS}   |{DQS}   |{DAS}   |{CRS}   |{MS}   |{PRS}

|Attribute entry values        |{y}     |{n}     |{n}     |{n}     |[3]    |{n}
|Comments                      |{n}     |{n}     |{n}     |{n}     |{n}    |{n}
|Examples                      |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}    |{y}
|Headers                       |{y}     | -      | -      |{n}     |{n}    |{n}
|Literal, listings, and source |{y}     |{n}     |{n}     |{n}     |{n}    |{n}
|Macros                        |{y}+[1] |{y}+[2] |{y}+[2] |{y}+[2] |{y}    |{y} + [2]
|Open                          |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}    |{y}
|Paragraphs                    |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}    |{y}
|Passthrough blocks            |{n}     |{n}     |{n}     |{n}     |{y}    |{n}
|Quotes and verses             |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}    |{y}
|Sidebars                      |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}    |{y}
|Tables                        |{y}     |Varies  |Varies  |Varies  |Varies |Varies
|Titles                        |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}     |{y}    |{y}
|=====================================
[1]:: (except triple plus and inline pass macros)
[2]:: (except passthrough macros)
[3]:: Only the Inline pass macro

å¼•ç”¨å†…å®¹æ›¿æ¢ï¼ˆQuotes Substitutionsï¼‰æ˜¯å†…è”å…ƒç´ ä¸Šçš„æ ¼å¼åŒ–æ›¿æ¢ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ä½¿ç”¨æ˜Ÿå·åŠ ç²—ï¼Œ
åœ¨è½¬æ¢ä¸º HTML è¾“å‡ºæ—¶æ›¿æ¢ä¸º `<strong>` æ ‡ç­¾ã€‚ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯å¼•ç”¨æ›¿æ¢å¯¹åº”çš„ HTML æ ¼å¼ï¼š

.HTML source code generated from AsciiDoc formatting syntax
[#table-quotes-html%autowidth,cols="~,^~,^~"]
|============================================
|Name                 |AsciiDoc     |HTML

|emphasis             |+_word_+     |<em>word</em>
|strong               |+*word*+     |<strong>word</strong>
|monospace            |+`word`+     |<code>word</code>
|superscript          |+^word^+     |<sup>word</sup>
|subscript            |+~word~+     |<sub>word</sub>
|double curved quotes |+"`word`"+   |+&#8220;word&#8221;+
|single curved quotes |+'`word`'+   |+&#8216;word&#8217;+
|============================================

å±æ€§æ›¿æ¢ï¼ˆAttributes substitutionï¼‰æ˜¯ä½¿ç”¨æ–‡æ¡£å±æ€§å€¼è¿›è¡Œå†…å®¹æ›¿æ¢ï¼Œè¯­æ³•æ ¼å¼ä½¿ç”¨èŠ±æ‹¬å·
åŒ…è£¹ä¸€ä¸ªå±æ€§åç§°ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ `+{docname}+` å°±æ˜¯ä½¿ç”¨ AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£åç§°ï¼ˆä¸å«æ‰©å±•åï¼‰æ›¿æ¢ã€‚

ç¬¦å·æ›¿æ¢ï¼ˆCharacter Replacement Substitutionsï¼‰æ˜¯æŒ‡ç”¨é”®ç›˜ä¸Šå¸¸è§å¯ç›´æ¥è¾“å…¥çš„
ä¸€äº›å­—ç¬¦æ›¿ä»£å…¶å®ƒä¸å¤ªæ˜“å®¹é€šè¿‡é”®ç›˜è¾“å…¥çš„ç¬¦å·ã€‚æ¯”å¦‚ç‰ˆæƒç¬¦å· Â© æˆ–æ³¨å†Œç¬¦å· Â®ï¼Œå°±å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨
+(C)+ å’Œ +(R)+ è¿™æ ·çš„å­—ç¬¦æ¥æ¨¡æ‹Ÿã€‚ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯æ–‡æœ¬ç¬¦å·æ›¿æ¢å…³ç³»è¡¨ï¼š

[%autowidth,cols="~,^~,^~,^~,~"]
.Textual symbol replacements
|===========================
|Name |Syntax |Unicode Replacement |Rendered |Notes

|Copyright               |+(C)+   |+&#169;+      |(C)   |
|Registered              |+(R)+   |+&#174;+      |(R)   |
|Trademark               |+(TM)+  |+&#8482;+     |(TM)  |
|Em dash                 |+--+    |+&#8212;+     |{empty}--{empty}
    |Only replaced if between two word characters, between a word 
    character and a line boundary, or flanked by spaces.

    When flanked by space characters (e.g., `+a -- b+`), the
    normal spaces are replaced by thin spaces (\&#8201;).

    Otherwise, the em dash is followed by a zero-width space 
    (\&#8203;) to provide a break opportunity.
|Ellipsis                |+...+   |+&#8230;+     |...
    |The ellipsis is followed by a zero-width space (\&#8203;) 
    to provide a break opportunity.
|Single right arrow      |+->+    |+&#8594;+     |->    |
|Double right arrow      |+=>+    |+&#8658;+     |=>    |
|Single left arrow       |+<-+    |+&#8592;+     |<-    |
|Double left arrow       |+<=+    |+&#8656;+     |<=    |
|Typographic apostrophe  |Sam\'s  |+Sam&#8217;s+ |Sam's
    |The typewriter apostrophe is replaced with the typographic 
    (aka curly or smart) apostrophe.
|===========================

AsciiDoc å®šä¹‰äº†ä»¥ä¸‹æ›¿æ¢åˆ†ç»„ï¼Œå„åˆ†ç»„ä¸æ›¿æ¢è§„åˆ™çš„å…³ç³»å¦‚ä¸‹:

.Substitution types used by each substitution group (cqarmp)
[#table-subs-groups,cols="1,6*^"]
:c: Special characters 
:q: Quotes 
:a: Attributes 
:r: Replacements 
:m: Macros 
:p: Post replacements
:y: pass:q[#Yes#]
:n: No
|===
|Group    |{c}  |{q}  |{a}  |{r}  |{m}  |{p}

|Header   |{y}  |{n}  |{y}  |{n}  |{n}  |{n} 
|None     |{n}  |{n}  |{n}  |{n}  |{n}  |{n} 
|Normal   |{y}  |{y}  |{y}  |{y}  |{y}  |{y} 
|Pass     |{n}  |{n}  |{n}  |{n}  |{n}  |{n} 
|Verbatim |{y}  |{n}  |{n}  |{n}  |{n}  |{n} 
|===

Normal substitution group::
  æ­£å¸¸æ›¿æ¢åˆ†ç»„ (`normal`) æ˜¯å¤§å¤šæ•° AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£å…ƒç´ çš„æ›¿æ¢é…ç½®ã€‚

Header substitution group::
  å¤´éƒ¨å…ƒæ•°æ®æ›¿æ¢åˆ†ç»„ (`header`) ç”¨äº metadata lines å†…å®¹æ›¿æ¢ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ï¼Œåœ¨æ–‡æ¡£å¤´éƒ¨ä¸­çš„
  ä½œè€… author æˆ–è€…ä¿®è®¢ç‰ˆæœ¬ revision ç­‰ä¿¡æ¯ã€‚ä¹Ÿåº”ç”¨äº document header æˆ–è€… body
  ä¸­å‡ºç°çš„ attribute entries å±æ€§å€¼ã€‚å¤´éƒ¨å…ƒç´ åˆ†ç»„ä¸­ä¼šå¯¹ special characters, attribute references ä»¥åŠå†…è”çš„ `pass` å®è¿›è¡Œæ›¿æ¢ã€‚å¯ä»¥åœ¨åœ¨å±æ€§å®ä½“ä¸­ä½¿ç”¨
  å†…è” `pass` å®æ¥ç»™å±æ€§å€¼åšç›´é€šå¤„ç†ã€‚æ¯”å¦‚ `:author: \pass:a,q[*{author}*]`ï¼Œ
  ä½†æ˜¯å†…ç½®çš„ `:docname:` å±æ€§å€¼å¹¶ä¸èƒ½è¿›è¡Œä¿®æ”¹ã€‚

Verbatim substitution group::
  å­—é¢é‡åŸæ ·åˆ†ç»„ (`verbatim`) é€‚ç”¨äº Literal, listing, source blocks ç­‰ç­‰
  éœ€è¦ä¿æŒå†…å®¹åŸæ ·è¾“å‡ºçš„å…ƒç´ ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”åªæœ‰ special characters ä¼šè¢«æ›¿æ¢ã€‚

Pass substitution group::
  ç›´é€šå†…å®¹åˆ†ç»„ (`pass`) ä¸ä¼šè¿›è¡Œå†…å®¹çš„æ›¿æ¢ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬ passthrough block, ä»¥åŠ
  inline pass macro å’Œ triple plus macroï¼Œä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯å†…è” `pass` å®çš„å„ç§å½¢å¼ï¼š
  `\pass:[...]`, `pass:[+...+]`, `pass:[++...++]`, `pass:[+++...+++]`ã€‚

None substitution group::
  éæ›¿æ¢å†…å®¹åˆ†ç»„ (`none`) åªç”¨äºæ³¨è§£å†…å®¹å—ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬å•è¡Œæ³¨è§£ï¼ˆ//ï¼‰ å’Œå—æ³¨è§£ï¼ˆ///ï¼‰ï¼Œ
  æ³¨è§£æ ‡è®°ç¬¦å·å¿…éœ€ä½äºè¡Œé¦–ï¼Œä¸æœ‰æœ‰å‰ç¼€ä»»ä½•å­—ç¬¦ï¼Œä¸èƒ½ä½äºå…¶å®ƒå†…å®¹åé¢ã€‚


æ¯ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ï¼Œblock æˆ–è€… inline å…ƒç´ éƒ½æœ‰é»˜è®¤çš„æ›¿æ¢åˆ†ç»„ï¼ˆsubstitution groupï¼‰ï¼Œ
è¿™æ˜¯ AsciiDoc å¤„ç†å™¨çš„è¿›è¡Œå®æ›¿æ¢çš„åŸºæœ¬åŠŸèƒ½ï¼Œåœ¨æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡å±æ€§é…ç½®æ›¿æ¢è¿‡ç¨‹ã€‚
æ›¿æ¢è¿‡ç¨‹æ˜¯ä»¥ group ç»„ç»‡çš„ï¼Œè®¾ç½® `subs` å±æ€§åï¼Œå°±ä¼šæ¸…é™¤é»˜è®¤çš„æ›¿æ¢åˆ†ç»„è®¾ç½®ï¼Œ
æ·»åŠ åˆ°åˆ†ç»„çš„æ›¿æ¢è§„åˆ™ç§°ä¸ºå¢é‡æ›¿æ¢æ­¥éª¤ï¼ˆincremental substitutions step)ã€‚
å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ + - å·ä¿®é¥°æ¥æ·»åŠ æˆ–è€…ç§»é™¤å¢é‡æ›¿æ¢æ­¥éª¤ï¼Œå¦åˆ™è®¾ç½®å°†æ›¿ä»£ç°æœ‰çš„æ›¿æ¢è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼š

* `<substitution>+`: Prepends the substitution to the default list.
* `+<substitution>`: Appends the substitution to the default list.
* `-<substitution>`: Removes the substitution from the default list.

NOTE: The `subs` element attribute does not inherit to nested blocks.
      It can only be applied to a leaf block, which is any block that cannot 
      have child blocks (e.g., a paragraph or a listing block).
      è¿™æ®µæ³¨è§£åŸæ–‡åœ¨æœªç†è§£ `subs` å«ä¹‰çš„å‰æä¸‹å¾ˆå®¹æ˜“é€ æˆé˜…è¯»ç†è§£è¯¯å·®ï¼Œå°†å…¶
      å½“ä½œä¸ºä¸€ä¸ª elementï¼Œä»è€Œå¯¼è‡´ç¬¬ä¸€å¥è¯çš„æ„æ€è¯¯è§£ä¸º â€œ`subs` å…ƒç´ çš„å±æ€§â€ã€‚
      æ›´æ¸…æ™°çš„è¡¨è¾¾å¯ä»¥æ¢æˆ â€œThe `subs` attribte of element...â€ã€‚

ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯ block å®æ›¿æ¢ä¸­è®¾ç½®æ›¿æ¢æ–¹å¼çš„å±æ€§è¡¨ï¼Œæ ¹æ®éœ€è¦è®¾ç½®åœ¨ `subs` å±æ€§ä¸­ï¼š

|============
| subs groups   | Notes

|`none`         |æ­¤åˆ†ç»„ç¦æ­¢ä¸€åˆ‡å†…å®¹æ›¿æ¢è¡Œä¸ºï¼Œå°±åƒæ³¨è§£å†…å®¹ä¸€æ ·åŸæ ·è¾“å‡ºï¼›

|`specialchars` |ç‰¹æ®Šå­—ç¬¦å¤„ç†ï¼Œæ›¿æ¢ `<`, `>`, `&` ç­‰ XML/HTML æ ‡è®°å­—ç¬¦ä¸ºå®ä½“åï¼ŒåŒç è¯­æ³•é«˜äº®ä¼šåå¤„ç†ã€‚

                 åŒ…æ‹¬å­—ç¬¦ entity, HTML ä¸ XML å­—ç¬¦å¼•ç”¨ã€‚è¾“å‡ºå†…å®¹å–å†³äºå‰ä¸€æ­¥æ‰§è¡Œçš„ `specialchars`ã€‚

[NOTE]
    æ³¨æ„ï¼Œå­—ç¬¦å¼•ç”¨ä¸äººç‰©æ¨èä¿¡ï¼ˆCharacter Reference Letterï¼‰æ˜¯å®Œå…¨ä¸åŒçš„å«ä¹‰ï¼Œ
    è™½ç„¶ä½¿ç”¨çš„å•è¯ç›¸åŒã€‚å­—ç¬¦å¼•ç”¨å‡†ç¡®è¯´æ˜¯å‘½åå­—ç¬¦çš„å¼•ç”¨ï¼ˆNamed character referencesï¼‰ï¼Œ
    å‘½åå­—ç¬¦æ˜¯é¿å…å­—ç¬¦æŒ‰åŸæ ·å‡ºç°æ—¶ä¸ HTML æˆ–è€… XML æ ‡è®°ç¬¦å·å†²çªè€Œé‡‡å–çš„ä¸€ç§é˜²å¾¡ã€‚

[TIP]
=====
æ³¨æ„ï¼Œå³ä½¿è®¾ç½® subs="none" ç¦æ­¢æ‰€æœ‰æ›¿æ¢è¡Œä¸ºï¼Œä½†æ˜¯ç”±äº Inline Preprocessor æ‰§è¡Œ
æ—¶æ‰€æ¶‰åŠçš„æ¡ä»¶é¢„å¤„ç†æŒ‡ä»¤å¹¶ä¸å±äºå†…å®¹æ›¿æ¢è¡Œä¸ºï¼Œä¹Ÿä¸å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡ä»¥ä¸Šé…ç½®æ¥å½±å“ã€‚æ‰€ä»¥ï¼Œåƒä»¥ä¸‹
ä»£ç ç‰‡æ®µï¼Œå³ä½¿ç¦æ­¢æ›¿æ¢è¡Œä¸ºï¼Œä½†æ˜¯å…¶ä¸­çš„ ifdef ç­‰ç­‰æŒ‡ä»¤è¿˜æ˜¯æœ‰æ•ˆåœ°è¿‡æ»¤ç‰¹å®šå†…å®¹ã€‚åªæ˜¯

.Matches a conditional preprocessor directive (e.g., ifdef, ifndef, ifeval and endif). {Ref}

== Document Attributes

åŒæ—¶å…¶å†…å®¹è¾“å‡ºä¹Ÿä¸ºç©ºã€‚å±æ€§å¸ƒå°”å€¼ `true` ä½¿ç”¨ç©ºå­—ç¬¦è¡¨ç¤ºï¼Œå³ `:name:` è¿™æ ·çš„å±æ€§è®¾ç½®ã€‚
æ³¨æ„ï¼Œæ²¡æœ‰åç¼€ä»»ä½•å­—ç¬¦ï¼Œç‹¬å ä¸€è¡Œã€‚ç”¨æˆ·æ²¡æœ‰è®¾ç½®çš„å±æ€§å°±åˆ¤æ–­ä¸º falseï¼Œé™¤äº†å†…ç½®å±æ€§ä»¥å¤–ã€‚

æ¸…é™¤å±æ€§è®¾ç½®ä½¿ç”¨ bang symbol (`!`)ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½œä¸ºå‰ç¼€ã€åç¼€ï¼Œ`:!name:` æˆ–è€… `:name!:`ã€‚

ç”¨æˆ·å®šä¹‰å±æ€§åç§°ç¬¦åˆå¸¸ç”¨æ ‡è¯†è§„åˆ™ï¼Œä¸èƒ½æœ‰å¥ç‚¹ç­‰ç¬¦å·ï¼š

* be at least one character long,
* begin with a word character (A-Z, a-z, 0-9, or _), and
* only contain word characters and hyphens.

å½“ä½¿ç”¨ç¼ºå°‘å®šä¹‰çš„å±æ€§æ—¶äº§ç”Ÿ Missing attribute è¡Œä¸ºï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ `attribute-missing`
å±æ€§æ¥è®¾ç½®å“åº”æ–¹å¼ï¼Œå‡è®¾æ–‡æ¡£ä½¿ç”¨äº†è¿™æ ·çš„å±æ€§å¼•ç”¨ `+Hello, {name}!+`ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”æ²¡æœ‰å®šä¹‰
`name` å±æ€§ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆå¤„ç†æ–¹å¼ä¸ç›¸åº”æ•ˆæœå¦‚ä¸‹è¡¨æ‰€ç¤ºã€‚å…¶ä¸­ `warn` æ–¹å¼è¾ƒç‰¹åˆ«ï¼Œå®ƒè¾“å‡ºå†…å®¹
å’Œ `skip` ä¸€æ ·ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯ä¼šåœ¨ AsciiDoctor æ§åˆ¶å°è¾“å‡ºè­¦å‘Šä¿¡æ¯ã€‚

[%autowidth]
|===
|`attribute-missing` value |Result

|`skip`      |Hello, \{name}!
|`drop`      |Hello, !
|`drop-line` |{empty}
|`warn`      |`asciidoctor: WARNING: skipping reference to missing attribute: XYZ`
|===

.Document header structure
[source,asciidoc]
----
= Document Title (1)
Jeango W. Yep <virtual@example.com>; Jimbo_Y M. Walt <other@example.com> (2)
v0.0.1, 2025-01-20: revision remark (3)
:author: Jeango (4)
:email: <virtual@example.com> (5)
:revnumber: 0.0.1 (6)
:revdate: 2025-01-20 (7)
:revremark: revision remark (8)
(9)
----

1. Optional document title
2. Optional author line
3. Optional revision info (version, date, remark - each optional); 
   only be used below the author line.
4. An alternative way to set the optional author name; see author info docs
5. An alternative way to set the optional author email
6. An alternative way to set the optional revision number (no 'v' prefix)
7. An alternative way to set the optional revision date
8. An alternative way to set the optional revision remark
9. Blank line that ends the document header

[[passthroughs]]

.Examples of Single plus, double plus and Triple plus passthrough
[cols="3"]
|===
|Strong (Bold) Subscript|Strong (Bold) + pass          |Plus passthroughs with +

|  *^{docname}^*        |  +*^<u>{docname}</u>^*+  (2) |  `+ +<u>*bold*</u>+ +`ï¼Œ
| **^{docname}^**       | ++*^<u>{docname}</u>^*++ (2) | `++ +<u>*bold*</u>+ ++`ï¼Œ
|***^{docname}^*** (1)  |+++*^<u>{docname}</u>^*+++(3) |`+++ ++<u>*bold*</u>++ +++`ï¼Œ
|===

.Examples of Single plus, double plus and Triple plus passthrough
[cols="3"]
|===
|Strong (Bold) Subscript|Strong (Bold) + pass          |Plus passthroughs with +

|  *^{docname}^*        |  +*^<u>{docname}</u>^*+  (2) |  `+ +<u>*bold*</u>+ +`ï¼Œ
| **^{docname}^**       | ++*^<u>{docname}</u>^*++ (2) | `++ +<u>*bold*</u>+ ++`ï¼Œ
|***^{docname}^*** (1)  |+++*^<u>{docname}</u>^*+++(3) |`+++ ++<u>*bold*</u>++ +++`ï¼Œ

.Substitution values accepted by the inline pass macro (cqarmp)
[cols=">1m,5",width=100%ï¼Œopts="autowidth"]
|=======================
h|Shorthand   h| Substitution Type

 |c            |Special Characters

 |p            |Post replacements

 |n            |Normal

|=======================

è·¨è¡Œæˆ–è·¨åˆ—ï¼ˆcolSpan, rowSpanï¼‰ç›´æ¥æŒ‡å®šæ•°å€¼ï¼Œå†…å®¹å¯¹é½ï¼ˆhAlignï¼ŒvAlignï¼‰ä½¿ç”¨ `<^>`

ä½¿ç”¨åŠ ç²—æ ·å¼ `s` (Strong)ã€‚

é€šå¸¸è¡¨å¤´ä¸­è®¾ç½®è¡¨æ ¼æœ‰è·¨åˆ—ï¼Œç”¨äºæ§åˆ¶å•å…ƒæ ¼å ç”¨çš„ç©ºé—´æ¯”ä¾‹ï¼Œè¡¨æ ¼å±æ€§é…ç½®åªè®¾ç½®ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å€¼è¡¨ç¤º

ç¬¬ä¸‰åˆ—å†…å®¹è¾ƒå¤šï¼Œåˆ†é…äº† 70% å®½åº¦ç©ºé—´ï¼Œ70% = 7/(2+1+7)ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥ä½¿ç”¨ % å•ä½è®¾ç½®ã€‚éœ€è¦

é™¤äº†ç›´æ¥ä½¿ç”¨ `cols` å±æ€§æŒ‡å®šè¡¨æ ¼åˆ—æ•°é‡ï¼ˆé€—å·åˆ†éš”åˆ—æˆ–è€…æ•°å€¼æŒ‡å®šåˆ—ï¼‰ï¼Œè¿˜å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨åˆ—ä¹˜æ•°ç¬¦å·

å°±ä¼šä½¿ç”¨éšå«åˆ—è®¾ç½®ï¼ˆimplicit colsï¼‰ï¼Œå³è¡¨ç¤ºç¬¬ä¸€è¡Œä½¿ç”¨ `|` ç¬¦å·è®¾ç½®çš„å•å…ƒæ ¼æ•°é‡ã€‚

.Style operators
[cols="4*^.^100%a"]
|===
2+|Cell span 2 collum   |Two +
                         line
                    1.2+|Cell span 2 rows
2.2+^.^|Cell span 2 collums and 2 rows (\(2 \times 2\))  
|*Mass-energy equation* \[e=mc^2\] 
|One cell of \(1 \times 1\)
|*Extra cell stem:[1 \times 1]*
|===

WARNING: è¡¨æ ¼åˆ—æ•°é‡ã€å•å…ƒæ ¼è·¨è¡Œè®¾ç½®éœ€è¦ä¸è¡¨æ ¼çš„å•å…ƒæ ¼æ•°æ®é‡è®¾ç½®ä¸€è‡´ï¼Œå½“è¡¨æ ¼æœ«ç«¯å•å…ƒæ ¼æ•°
ä¸è¶³ä¸€è¡Œæ—¶ï¼Œä¼šè¢«ç›´æ¥ä¸¢å¼ƒã€‚å¦‚æœè·¨åˆ—ä¸è¡Œå•å…ƒæ ¼æ•°é‡ä¸åŒ¹é…æ—¶ï¼Œæ•´ä¸ªè¡¨æ ¼æ— æ•ˆï¼Œä¸æ¸²æŸ“ã€‚

.Style operators
[cols="2d,1e,7"]
|===
|Style     |Operator |Description

s|AsciiDoc |`a` |Supports block elements (lists, delimited blocks, and block macros).
                 This style effectively creates a nested, standalone AsciiDoc document.
                 The parent document's implicit attributes, such as `doctitle`, 
                 are shadowed and custom attributes are inherited.
// what does "shadowed" actually mean???
|Default   |`d` |All of the markup that is permitted in a paragraph 
                 (i.e., inline formatting, inline macros) is supported.
|Emphasis  |`e` |Text is italicized.
|Header    |`h` |Applies the header semantics and styles to the text and cell borders.
|Literal   |`l` |Content is treated as if it were inside a literal block.
|Monospace |`m` |Text is rendered using a monospace font.
|Strong    |`s` |Text is bold.
|Verse     |`v` |the verse operator `v` has been deprecated
|===

https://docs.asciidoctor.org/asciidoc/latest/tables[Table `frame`, `grid`, `stripes`]
å‡ ä¸ªæ˜¯ç”¨äºæ§åˆ¶è¡¨æ ¼æ„æ¶ä¸å•å…ƒæ ¼è¾¹æ¡†ä»¥åŠè¡Œæ–¹å‘æ¡å¸¦çš„å±æ€§ï¼Œå®ƒä»¬çš„å¯é€‰å€¼ä¸ºï¼š

[cols=">,<,",opts="autowidth,header"]
[frame=sides,grid=rows,stripes=even,rotate]
|====
|attribute |document attribute |values (default in bold)
|`frame`   | `table-frame`     |*`all`*, `ends`, `sides` or `none`.
|`grid`    | `table-grid`      |*`all`*, `rows`, `cols` or `none`.
|`stripes` | `table-stripes`  a|
  * *`none`* - no rows are shaded (default)
  * `even`  - even rows are shaded
  * `odd`   - odd rows are shaded
  * `all`   - all rows are shaded
  * `hover` - the row under the mouse cursor is shaded (HTML only)
|====

[source,asciidoc]
-----------------
[cols=">,<,",opts="autowidth,header"]
[frame=sides,grid=rows,stripes=even,rotate]
|====
|attribute |document attribute |values (default in bold)
|`frame`   | `table-frame`     |*`all`*, `ends`, `sides` or `none`.
|`grid`    | `table-grid`      |*`all`*, `rows`, `cols` or `none`.
|`stripes` | `table-stripes`  a|
  * *`none`* - no rows are shaded (default)
  * `even`  - even rows are shaded
  * `odd`   - odd rows are shaded
  * `all`   - all rows are shaded
  * `hover` - the row under the mouse cursor is shaded (HTML only)
|====
-----------------

DocBook æ”¯æŒä½¿ç”¨ `orientation=landscape`ï¼Œç®€å†™ `orient=land` æˆ–è€… `rotate` ä½¿ç”¨è¡¨æ ¼
é€†æ—¶é’ˆæ—‹è½¬ 90Â°ã€‚å¦å¤– AsciiDoc æ”¯æŒé€šè¿‡æ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ï¼ˆCSV, TSV, DSV Dataï¼‰æ¥ç”Ÿæˆè¡¨æ ¼ã€‚ç”±äºä¸åŒ
æ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­çš„æ•°æ®ç»“æ„ä½¿ç”¨ä¸åŒçš„åˆ†éš”ç¬¦å·ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥æä¾›äº† `separator` å±æ€§æ¥æŒ‡å®šè‡ªå®šä¹‰çš„è¡¨æ ¼å•å…ƒåˆ†éš”
ç¬¦å·ï¼Œä¾‹å¦‚ä½¿ç”¨ Unicode Â¦ - é—´æ–­æ¡ (Broken vertical bar)ã€‚

The Piano Guys:Code Name Vivaldi:Classical

æŒ‰ç…§ Section Styles for Articles and Books (sections/pages/styles.adoc)
æ–‡æ¡£æ‰€è¿°ï¼Œä¸€èˆ¬æ¨¡å¼å’Œ `:doctype: book` æ¨¡æ‹Ÿä¸‹å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ä»¥ä¸‹ç‰¹æ®Šçš„æ–‡æ¡£åˆ†åŒºç±»å‹ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨æ—¶
åªéœ€è¦ç”¨æ–¹æ‹¬å·åŒ…è£¹å¹¶ç½®äºæ ‡é¢˜å‰é¢ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ `[appendix]` å¯ä»¥æ ‡è®°ä¸€ä¸ªé™„å½•ç« èŠ‚åˆ†åŒºï¼š

.Section styles
|===
| :doctype: book | :doctype: article
a| *front*

* _abstract_ (becomes a chapter)
* colophon
* dedication
* acknowledgments
* preface
* partintro (must be first child of part)

*back*

* _appendix_
* _glossary_
* _bibliography_
* _index_

a| *front*

* abstract

*back*

* appendix
* glossary
* bibliography
* index
|===

ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ª AsciiDoc æ–‡æ¡£å¤§çº²æ¨¡æ¿å‚è€ƒï¼š

.An adoc outline
----------------
  = AsciiDoc Outline
  :doctype: book
  :partnums:
  :toc:
  :toclevels: 3
  :sectnumlevels: 3
  :sectnums: |,all|
  :part-signifier: Part
  :chapter-signifier: C.
  :chapter-refsig: Ch.
  :section-refsig: Sec.
  :appendix-refsig: App.

  [abstract]
  == Abstract

  æ–‡æ¡£å¤§çº²ç»“æ„å‚è€ƒï¼šAsciiDoc Language Specification Outline 
  footnote:[æ–‡æ¡£æ–‡ä»¶å spec/outline.adoc]

  æ–‡æ¡£æ ‡é¢˜åˆ†åŒºå‚è€ƒï¼šSection Styles for Articles and Books 
  footnote:[æ–‡æ¡£æ–‡ä»¶å sections/pages/styles.adoc]

  indexterm:[Index, "User Index"]

  xref:c1[xrefstyle=full] |xref:s1[xrefstyle=full] | xref:a1[xrefstyle=short]

  {doctype}

  = Outline Part
  :doctype: article

  {doctype}

[[diabolical_mathematical_opus]]
== Diabolical Mathematical Opus

// Activating STEM support
:stem: latex

AsciiDoc æ•°å­¦å…¬å¼æ”¯æŒåŠŸèƒ½ç§°ä¸º Science, Technology, Engineering and Math (STEM) ï¼Œ
éœ€è¦åœ¨æ–‡æ¡£å¤´é…ç½® `:stem:` æ¿€æ´»æ•°å­¦å…¬å¼å†…å®¹è§£é‡Šï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ AsciiMath æˆ–è€… \(\LaTeX\) å…¬å¼ã€‚
å¯¹åº”ä¸º `:stem: asciimath` å’Œ `:stem: latex`ï¼Œæ²¡æœ‰æŒ‡æ˜å…¬å¼æ¸²æŸ“ç±»å‹ï¼Œåˆ™é»˜è®¤ AsciiMathã€‚
å¦‚æœä½¿ç”¨ AsciiMath æ¸²æŸ“ \(\LaTeX\) å…¬å¼ç¬¦å·ï¼Œä¼šåœ¨å…¬å¼çš„å‰åæ˜¾ç¤º `\$` è¿™ä¸ªå…¸å‹çš„å­—ç¬¦æ ‡è®°ã€‚
è¿˜å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ `\( ... \)` æˆ– `\[ ... \]` ä½œä¸ºåŒ…è£¹æ•°å­¦å…¬å¼çš„æ ‡è®°ï¼Œå‰è€…æ˜¯å†…è”å½¢å¼ï¼Œåè€…æ˜¯å—æ¨¡å¼ã€‚
è¿˜å¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥ä½¿ç”¨ \(\LaTeX\) å…¬å¼ç¬¦å·æ¥åŒ…è£¹å…¬å¼ï¼Œ`\begin` ä»¥åŠ `\end` ï¼Œä»¥ä¸‹å°±ä»¥çŸ©é˜µç¬¦å·
ï¼ˆ`\begin{pmatrix}`ã€`\end{pmatrix}`ï¼‰ï¼Œç¼–å·å…¬å¼ï¼ˆ`\begin{equation}`ã€`\end{equation}`ï¼‰ï¼Œ
ä»¥åŠå…¬å¼å¯¹é½ï¼ˆ`\begin{aligned}`ã€`\end{aligned}`ï¼‰ ç­‰ç­‰ç¬¦å·ï¼Œæ¼”ç¤ºç›´æ¥ä½¿ç”¨  \(\LaTeX\)
å…¬å¼ç¬¦å·æ¥åŒ…è£¹å…¬å¼å†…å®¹ï¼š

[stem]
++++++
\begin{aligned}
\mathbb{G} &= \begin{pmatrix}a && x\\b && y\\c && z\end{pmatrix} \\

\bar{C}_{result} &= \begin{pmatrix}
\color{red}{0.0} \\ \color{green}{1.0} \\ \color{blue}{0.0} \\ \color{purple}{0.6} 
\end{pmatrix} * \color{green}{0.6} +
\begin{pmatrix} 
\color{red}{1.0} \\ \color{green}{0.0} \\ \color{blue}{0.0} \\ \color{purple}{1.0}
\end{pmatrix} *
(\color{red}{1 - 0.6}) 
\end{aligned}
++++++

[source,asciidoc]
-----------------
// inline equation
stem:[\mathbb{G} = \begin{pmatrix}a && x\\b && y\\c && z\end{pmatrix}]

// block equation (center)
[stem]
++++++
\mathbb{G} = \begin{pmatrix}a && x\\b && y\\c && z\end{pmatrix}
++++++

// direct equations via LaTeX symbols
\begin{equation}
\bar{C}_{result} = \begin{pmatrix}
\color{red}{0.0} \\ \color{green}{1.0} \\ \color{blue}{0.0} \\ \color{purple}{0.6} 
\end{pmatrix} * \color{green}{0.6} +
\begin{pmatrix} 
\color{red}{1.0} \\ \color{green}{0.0} \\ \color{blue}{0.0} \\ \color{purple}{1.0}
\end{pmatrix} *
(\color{red}{1 - 0.6}) \end{equation}

\begin{equation} \label{eq1}
\begin{split}
A & = \frac{\pi r^2}{2} \\
  & = \frac{1}{2} \pi r^2
\end{split}
\end{equation}

æ–¹æ‹¬å·å¤–ä¾§ã€‚æ¯”å¦‚ `pass:[++]\(\LaTeX\)pass:[++]` æˆ–è€… `pass:[++]\[\LaTeX\]pass:[++]`ã€‚

Github æ”¯æŒæ•°å­¦å…¬å¼æ¸²æŸ“ï¼ˆlink:https://github.com/github/markup[markup]ï¼‰ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯ä¸æ”¯æŒæ³¨å…¥æ ·å¼
è¿™ç§é«˜å±è¡Œä¸ºã€‚AsciiDoc çš„æ•°å­¦å…¬å¼çš„ç¼–å†™ä¹Ÿæœ‰è¯­æ³•å·®å¼‚ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨ $ ç¬¦å·æˆ–è€… `pass:[```math\n...\n```]`
ä»£ç å—åŒ…è£¹å…¬å¼å†…å®¹ã€‚ä½†æ˜¯è¿™å‡ ç§æ–¹å¼ä¸ AsciiDoc.js ä¸å…¼å®¹ã€‚å…·ä½“å‚è€ƒå®˜æ–¹æ–‡æ¡£ï¼š

[source,markdown]
-----------------
This sentence uses `$` delimiters to show math inline: $\sqrt{3x-1}+(1+x)^2$

This sentence uses $\` and \`$ delimiters to show math inline: $`\sqrt{3x-1}+(1+x)^2`$

**The Cauchy-Schwarz Inequality**\

$$\left( \sum_{k=1}^n a_k b_k \right)^2 \leq \left( \sum_{k=1}^n a_k^2 \right) \left( \sum_{k=1}^n b_k^2 \right)$$

**The Cauchy-Schwarz Inequality**

```math
\left( \sum_{k=1}^n a_k b_k \right)^2 \leq \left( \sum_{k=1}^n a_k^2 \right) \left( \sum_{k=1}^n b_k^2 \right)
```
-----------------


å„ç§æ•°å­¦ç¬¦å·çš„ä½¿ç”¨å¯ä»¥å‚è€ƒ reStructuredText æä¾›çš„å‚è€ƒæ‰‹å†Œï¼š

https://www.mathjax.org[MathJax] and http://docs.mathjax.org[Docs] +
https://docutils.sourceforge.io/docs/ref/rst/mathematics.html[LaTeX syntax for mathematics] +
https://docs.asciidoctor.org/asciidoc/latest/stem/[Equations and Formulas (STEM)] +
https://docs.asciidoctor.org/asciidoctor/latest/stem/[AsciiDoctor STEM Processing]

ä»¥ä¸‹æ˜¯æ‘˜æŠ„ AsciiDoc Language Specification Outline - Blocks - STEM è¯´æ˜å†…å®¹ï¼š

* `pass:[++++]` block delimiter
* `stem` style if `stem` document attribute is set and has a value, otherwise `latexmath` or `asciimath`
* if block is empty, content should be empty string (not null)
* content model: pass, with some processing as required by STEM adapter


ä½¿ç”¨ `stem` å—ï¼ˆé…åˆç›´é€šåˆ†ç•Œï¼‰æˆ–è€…å†…è”å®æ—¶ï¼ŒAsciiDoc ä¼šå°†å…¬å¼å†…å®¹ç›´é€šè¾“å‡ºï¼Œç„¶ååœ¨å¯ç”¨å…¬å¼
æ¸²æŸ“å™¨çš„æ¡ä»¶ä¸‹å°†å…¬å¼ä»£ç æ¸²æŸ“ä¸ºå¯é˜…è¯»çš„æ•°å­¦è¯­è¨€ç¬¦å·ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚ï¼Œ`\stem:[Î±^0 = Îµ]` è¿™æ ·çš„å†…è”å…¬å¼
å°±ä¼šç›´é€šå¹¶æ·»åŠ  LaTeX çš„åŒ…è£¹ç¬¦å·å¾—åˆ° `\$Î±^0 = Îµ\$`ï¼Œå†å°†å®ƒäº¤ç»™å…¬å¼æ¸²æŸ“ç¨‹åºè½¬æ¢ä¸ºå¯é˜…è¯»å½¢å¼ã€‚
STEM Processing æ–‡æ¡£è¯´æ˜äº†åœ¨ä¸åŒç¯å¢ƒä¸­çš„æ•°å­¦å…¬å¼æ¸²æŸ“æ‰€ä¾èµ–çš„å·¥å…·ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ `\{backend}`
æµ‹è¯•å½“å‰å‰ç¯å¢ƒçš„åç«¯ç±»å‹ã€‚VS Code ä¸Šä¼šæ˜¾ç¤º webview-html5ï¼š

.STEM integrations (`{backend}`)
[cols="3,3,1,2",opts=autowidth]
|=====
| Library Name          | Supported Versions | Backends | Loaded By

| MathJax                  | 2.7.9           |  html    | client
| Asciidoctor Mathematical | 0.3.5           |  any     | processor
| AsciiMath (Ruby)         | 1.0.x or 2.0.x  |  docbook | processor
|=====

Inline stem macro syntax::
    latexmath:[\alpha(t_i)] +
    stem:[\sqrt{4} = 2]  +
    Water (stem:[H_2O]) is a critical component. +
    A matrix stem:[[[a,b\],[c,d\]\]((n),(k))].

----------
    latexmath:[\alpha(t_i)] +
    stem:[\sqrt{4} = 2]  +
    Water (stem:[H_2O]) is a critical component. +
    A matrix stem:[[[a,b\],[c,d\]\]((n),(k))].
----------

Block STEM content::

.An e-xciting limit with LaTeX!
[stem]
++++
\lim_{n \to \infty}\frac{n}{\sqrt[n]{n!}} = {\large e}
++++

.A basic square root with AsciiMath::
[asciimath]
++++
sqrt(4) = 2
++++

++++

.A basic square root with AsciiMath::
[asciimath]
++++
sqrt(4) = 2
++++

\dot{z} & = -\beta z + xyp
